{ArthaŚ, 1, 1}
{ArthaŚ, 1, 2}
ānvīkṣikī trayī vārttā daṇḍanītiśceti vidyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 1.1]
trayī vārttā daṇḍanītiśceti mānavāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 2.1]
trayīviśeṣo hyānvīkṣikīti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 3.1]
vārttā daṇḍanītiśceti bārhaspatyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 4.1]
saṃvaraṇamātraṃ hi trayī lokayātrāvida iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 5.1]
daṇḍanītir ekā vidyetyauśanasāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 6.1]
tasyāṃ hi sarvavidyārambhāḥ pratibaddhā iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 7.1]
catasra eva vidyā iti kauṭilyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 8.1]
tābhir dharmārthau yad vidyāt tad vidyānāṃ vidyātvam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 9.1]
sāṃkhyaṃ yogo lokāyataṃ cetyānvīkṣikī | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 10.1]
dharmādharmau trayyām arthānarthau vārttāyāṃ nayānayau daṇḍanītyāṃ balābale ca etāsāṃ hetubhir anvīkṣamāṇā lokasya upakaroti vyasane 'bhyudaye ca buddhim avasthāpayati prajñāvākyakriyāvaiśāradyaṃ ca karoti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 11.1]
pradīpaḥ sarvavidyānām upāyaḥ sarvakarmaṇām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 12.1]
āśrayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ śaśvad ānvīkṣikī matā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 2 12.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 3}
sāma ṛc yajurvedāḥ trayaḥ trayī | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463381_1]
atharvaveda itihāsavedau ca vedāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463382_1]
śikṣā kalpaḥ vyākaraṇam niruktam chandovicitiḥ jyotiṣam iti ca aṅgāni | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463383_1]
eṣa trayī dharmaḥ caturṇām varṇānām āśramāṇām ca svadharma sthāpanāt aupakārikaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463384_1]
svadharmaḥ brāhmaṇasya adhyayanam adhyāpanam yajanam yājanam dānam pratigrahaḥ ca kṣatriyasya adhyayanam yajanam dānam śastra ājīvaḥ bhūta rakṣaṇam ca vaiśyasya adhyayanam yajanam dānam kṛṣi pāśupālye vaṇijyā ca śūdrasya dvijāti śuśrūṣā vārttā kāru kuśīlava karma ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463385_1]
gṛhasthasya svadharma ājīvaḥ tulyaiḥ asamāna ṛṣibhiḥ vaivāhyam ṛtugāmi tvam deva pitṛ atithi pūjā bhṛtyeṣu tyāgaḥ śeṣa bhojanam ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463389_1]
brahmacāriṇaḥ svādhyāyaḥ agni kārya abhiṣekau bhaikṣa vrati tvam ācārye prāṇāntikā vṛttiḥ tad abhāve guru putre sabrahmacāriṇi _ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463390_1]
vānaprasthasya brahmacaryam bhūmau śayyā jaṭā ajina dhāraṇam agni hotra abhiṣekau devatā pitṛ atithi pūjā vanyaḥ ca āhāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463391_1]
parivrājakasya jita indriya tvam anārambhaḥ niṣkiṃcana tvam saṅga tyāgaḥ bhaikṣa vratam anekatra araṇye ca vāsaḥ bāhya abhyantaram ca śaucam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463392_1]
sarveṣām ahiṃsā satyam śaucam anasūyā ānṛśaṃsyam kṣamā ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463393_1]
svadharmaḥ svargāya ānantyāya ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463394_1]
tasya atikrame lokaḥ saṃkarāt ucchidyeta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463395_1]
tasmāt svadharmam bhūtānām rājā na vyabhicārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463396_1]
svadharmam saṃdadhānaḥ hi pretya ca iha ca nandati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463397_1]
vyavasthita ārya maryādaḥ kṛta varṇa āśrama sthitiḥ trayyā abhirakṣitaḥ lokaḥ prasīdati na sīdati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 3 463399_1]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 4}
kṛṣi pāśupālye vaṇijyā ca vārttā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463400_1]
dhānya paśu hiraṇya kupya viṣṭi pradānāt aupakārikā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463400_2]
tayā sva pakṣam para pakṣam ca vaśīkaroti kośa daṇḍābhyām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463401_1]
ānvīkṣikī trayī vārttānām yogakṣema sādhanaḥ daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463402_1]
tasya nītiḥ daṇḍanītiḥ a labdha lābha arthā labdha parirakṣaṇā rakṣita vivardhanā vṛddhasya tīrthe pratipādanā ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463402_2]
tasyām āyattā lokayātrā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463403_1]
tasmāt lokayātrā arthī nityam udyata daṇḍaḥ syāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463404_1]
na hi evaṃvidham vaśa upanayanam asti bhūtānām yathā daṇḍaḥ iti ācāryāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463406_1]
na iti kauṭilyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463407_1]
tīkṣṇa daṇḍaḥ hi bhūtānām udvejanīyaḥ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463408_1]
mṛdu daṇḍaḥ paribhūyate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463409_1]
yathārha daṇḍaḥ pūjyate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463410_1]
su vijñāta praṇītaḥ daṇḍaḥ prajāḥ dharma artha kāmaiḥ yojayati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463411_1]
duṣpraṇītaḥ kāma krodhābhyām avajñānāt _ vānaprastha parivrājakān api kopayati kim aṅga punar gṛhasthān | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463412_1]
a praṇītaḥ tu mātsya nyāyam udbhāvayati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463413_1]
balīyāḥ abalam hi grasate daṇḍadhara abhāve | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463414_1]
saḥ tena guptaḥ prabhavati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463415_1]
catur varṇa āśramaḥ lokaḥ rājñā daṇḍena pālitaḥ svadharma karma abhirataḥ vartate sveṣu vartmasu | [ArthaŚ, 1, 4 463417_1]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 5}
tasmāt daṇḍa mūlāḥ tisraḥ vidyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463418_1]
vinaya mūlaḥ daṇḍaḥ prāṇabhṛtām yogakṣema āvahaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463419_1]
kṛtakaḥ svābhāvikaḥ ca vinayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463420_1]
kriyā hi dravyam vinayati na adravyam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463421_1]
śuśrūṣā śravaṇa grahaṇa dhāraṇa vijñāna ūha apoha tattva abhiniviṣṭa buddhim vidyā vinayati na itaram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463422_1]
vidyānām tu yathāsvam ācārya prāmāṇyāt vinayaḥ niyamaḥ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463423_1]
vṛtta caula karmā lipim saṃkhyānam ca upayuñjīta vṛtta upanayanaḥ trayīm ānvīkṣikīm ca śiṣṭebhyaḥ vārttām adhyakṣebhyaḥ daṇḍanītim vaktṛ prayoktṛbhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463424_1]
brahmacaryam ca ṣoḍaśāt varṣāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463426_1]
atas godānam dārakarma ca asya | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463427_1]
nityaḥ ca vidyā vṛddha saṃyogaḥ vinaya vṛddhi artham tad mūla tvāt vinayasya | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463428_1]
pūrvam ahar bhāgam hasti aśva ratha praharaṇa vidyāsu vinayam gacchet paścimam itihāsa śravaṇe | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463429_1]
purāṇam itivṛttam ākhyāyikā udāharaṇam dharmaśāstram arthaśāstram ca iti itihāsaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463431_1]
śeṣam ahorātra bhāgam apūrva grahaṇam gṛhīta paricayam ca kuryāt a gṛhītānām ābhīkṣṇya śravaṇam ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463432_1]
śrutāt hi prajñā upajāyate prajñāyāḥ yogaḥ yogāt ātmavat tā iti vidyānām sāmarthyam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463433_1]
vidyā vinītaḥ rājā hi prajānām vinaye rataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463434_1]
ananyām pṛthivīm bhuṅkte sarva bhūta hite rataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 5 463435_1]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 6}
vidyā vinayahetur indriyajayaḥ kāmakrodhalobhamānamadaharṣatyāgāt kāryaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 1.1]
karṇatvagakṣijihvāghrāṇendriyāṇāṃ śabdasparśarūparasagandheṣvavipratipattir indriyajayaḥ śāstrānuṣṭhānaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 2.1]
kṛtsnaṃ hi śāstram idam indriyajayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 3.1]
tadviruddhavṛttir avaśyendriyaś cāturanto api rājā sadyo vinaśyati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 4.1]
yathā dāṇḍakyo nāma bhojaḥ kāmād brāhmaṇakanyām abhimanyamānaḥ sabandhurāṣṭro vinanāśa karālaśca vaidehaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 5.1]
kopājjanamejayo brāhmaṇeṣu vikrāntaḥ tālajaṅghaśca bhṛguṣu | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 6.1]
lobhād ailaścāturvarṇyam atyāhārayamāṇaḥ sauvīraścājabinduḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 7.1]
mānād rāvaṇaḥ paradārān aprayacchan duryodhano rājyād aṃśaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 7.2]
madād dambhodbhavo bhūtāvamānī haihayaścārjunaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 8.1]
harṣād vātāpir agastyam atyāsādayan vṛṣṇisaṃghaśca dvaipāyanam iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 9.1]
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ śatruṣaḍvargam āśritāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 10.1]
sabandhurāṣṭrā rājāno vineśur ajitendriyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 10.2]
śatruṣaḍvargam utsṛjya jāmadagnyo jitendriyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 11.1]
ambarīṣaśca nābhāgo bubhujāte ciraṃ mahīm | [ArthaŚ, 1, 6 11.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 7}
tasmāt ari ṣaḍvarga tyāgena indriya jayam kurvīta vṛddha saṃyogena prajñām cāreṇa cakṣuḥ utthānena yogakṣema sādhanam kārya anuśāsanena svadharma sthāpanam vinayam vidyā upadeśena loka priya tvam artha saṃyogena hitena vṛttim | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463450_1]
evam vaśya indriyaḥ para strī dravya hiṃsāḥ ca varjayet svapnam laulyam anṛtam uddhata veṣa tvam anarthya saṃyogam adharma saṃyuktam anartha saṃyuktam ca vyavahāram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463451_1]
dharma artha avirodhena kāmam seveta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463452_1]
na niḥsukhaḥ syāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463452_2]
samam _ trivargam anyonya anubaddham | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463453_1]
ekaḥ hi _ āsevitaḥ dharma artha kāmānām ātmānam itarau ca pīḍayati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463454_1]
arthaḥ eva pradhānaḥ iti kauṭilyaḥ artha mūlau hi dharma kāmau iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463455_1]
maryādām sthāpayet ācāryān amātyān _ ye enam apāya sthānebhyaḥ vārayeyuḥ chāyā nālikā pratodena _ rahasi pramādyantam abhitudeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463457_1]
sahāya sādhyam rāja tvam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463458_1]
cakram ekam na vartate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463458_2]
kurvīta sacivān tasmāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463459_1]
teṣām ca śṛṇuyāt matam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 7 463459_2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 8}
sahādhyāyinaḥ amātyān kurvīta dṛṣṭa śauca sāmarthya tvāt iti bhāradvājaḥ te hi asya viśvāsyāḥ bhavanti iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463460_1]
na iti viśālākṣaḥ saha krīḍita tvāt paribhavanti enam ye hi asya guhya sadharmāṇaḥ tān amātyān kurvīta samāna śīla vyasana tvāt te hi asya marma jña bhayāt na aparādhyanti iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463462_1]
sādhāraṇaḥ eṣa doṣaḥ iti pārāśarāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463466_1]
teṣām api marma jña bhayāt kṛta a kṛtāni anuvarteta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463467_1]
yāvadbhyaḥ guhyam ācaṣṭe janebhyaḥ puruṣa adhipaḥ avaśaḥ karmaṇā tena vaśyaḥ bhavati tāvatām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463469_1]
ye enam āpatsu prāṇa ābādha yuktāsu anugṛhṇīyuḥ tān amātyān kurvīta dṛṣṭa anurāga tvāt iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463470_1]
na iti piśunaḥ bhaktiḥ eṣā na buddhi guṇaḥ saṃkhyāta artheṣu karmasu niyuktāḥ ye yathā ādiṣṭam artham sa viśeṣam _ kuryuḥ tān amātyān kurvīta dṛṣṭa guṇa tvāt iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463471_1]
na iti kauṇapadantaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463474_1]
anyaiḥ amātya guṇaiḥ a yuktāḥ hi ete | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463475_1]
pitṛpaitāmahān amātyān kurvīta dṛṣṭa avadāna tvāt te hi enam apacarantam api na tyajanti sagandha tvāt a mānuṣeṣu api ca etat dṛśyate gāvaḥ hi a sagandham go gaṇam atikramya sagandheṣu eva avatiṣṭhante iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463476_1]
na iti vātavyādhiḥ te hi asya sarvam avagṛhya svāmi vat pracaranti tasmāt nīti vidaḥ navān amātyān kurvīta navāḥ tu yama sthāne daṇḍadharam manyamānāḥ na aparādhyanti iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463480_1]
na iti bāhudanti putraḥ śāstra vid a dṛṣṭa karmā karmasu viṣādam gacchet tasmāt abhijana prajñā śauca śaurya anurāga yuktān amātyān kurvīta guṇa prādhānyāt iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463484_1]
sarvam upapannam iti kauṭilyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463487_1]
kārya sāmarthyāt hi puruṣa sāmarthyam kalpyate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463488_1]
sāmarthyāt ca vibhajya amātya vibhavam deśa kālau ca karma ca amātyāḥ sarve eva ete kāryāḥ syuḥ na tu mantriṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 8 463490_1]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 9}
jānapado 'bhijātaḥ svavagrahaḥ kṛtaśilpaścakṣuṣmān prājño dhārayiṣṇur dakṣo vāgmī pragalbhaḥ pratipattimān utsāhaprabhāvayuktaḥ kleśasahaḥ śucir maitro dṛḍhabhaktiḥ śīlabalārogyasattvayuktaḥ stambhacāpalahīnaḥ sampriyo vairāṇām akartetyamātyasampat | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 1.1]
ataḥ pādārdhaguṇahīnau madhyamāvarau | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 2.1]
teṣāṃ janapadabhijanam avagrahaṃ cāptataḥ parīkṣeta samānavidyebhyaḥ śilpaṃ śāstracakṣuṣmattāṃ ca karmārambheṣu prajñāṃ dhārayiṣṇutāṃ dākṣyaṃ ca kathāyogeṣu vāgmitvaṃ prāgalbhyaṃ pratibhānavattvaṃ ca saṃvāsibhyaḥ śīlabalārogyasattvayogam astambham acāpalaṃ ca pratyakṣataḥ sampriyatvam avairatvaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 3.1]
pratyakṣaparokṣānumeyā hi rājavṛttiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 4.1]
svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 5.1]
paropadiṣṭaṃ parokṣam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 6.1]
karmasu kṛtenākṛtāvekṣaṇam anumeyam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 7.1]
yaugapadyāt tu karmaṇām anekatvād anekasthatvācca deśakālātyayo mā bhūd iti parokṣam amātyaiḥ kārayedityamātyakarma | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 8.1]
purohitam uditoditakulaśīlaṃ sāṅge vede daive nimitte daṇḍanītyāṃ cābhivinītam āpadāṃ daivamānuṣīṇām atharvabhir upāyaiśca pratikartāraṃ kurvīta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 9.1]
tam ācāryaṃ śiṣyaḥ pitaraṃ putro bhṛtyaḥ svāminam iva cānuvarteta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 10.1]
brāhmaṇenaidhitaṃ kṣatraṃ mantrimantrābhimantritam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 11.1]
jayatyajitam atyantaṃ śāstrānugamaśastritam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 9 11.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 10}
mantripurohitasakhaḥ sāmānyeṣvadhikaraṇeṣu sthāpayitvāmātyān upadhābhiḥ śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 1.1]
purohitam ayājyayājanādhyāpane niyuktam amṛṣyamāṇaṃ rājāvakṣipet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 2.1]
sa sattribhiḥ śapathapūrvam ekaikam amātyam upajāpayet adhārmiko 'yaṃ rājā sādhu dhārmikam anyam asya tatkulīnam aparuddhaṃ kulyam ekapragrahaṃ sāmantam āṭavikam aupapādikaṃ vā pratipādayāmaḥ sarveṣām etad rocate kathaṃ vā tava iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 3.1]
pratyākhyāne śuciḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 4.1]
iti dharmopadhā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 4.2]
senāpatir asatpragraheṇāvakṣiptaḥ sattribhir ekaikam amātyam upajāpayet lobhanīyenārthena rājavināśāya sarveṣām etad rocate kathaṃ vā tava iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 5.1]
pratyākhyāne śuciḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 6.1]
ityarthopadhā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 6.2]
parivrājikā labdhaviśvāsāntaḥpure kṛtasatkārā mahāmātram ekaikam upajapet rājamahiṣī tvāṃ kāmayate kṛtasamāgamopāyā mahān arthaśca te bhaviṣyati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 7.1]
pratyākhyāne śuciḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 8.1]
iti kāmopadhā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 8.2]
prahavaṇanimittam eko 'mātyaḥ sarvān amātyān āvāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 9.1]
tenodvegena rājā tān avarundhyāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 10.1]
kāpaṭikaścātra pūrvāvaruddhasteṣām arthamānāvakṣiptam ekaikam amātyam upajapet asatpravṛtto 'yaṃ rājā sādhvenaṃ hatvānyaṃ pratipādayāmaḥ sarveṣām etad rocate kathaṃ vā tava iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 11.1]
pratyākhyāne śuciḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 12.1]
iti bhayopadhā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 12.2]
tatra dharmopadhāśuddhān dharmasthīyakaṇṭakaśodhaneṣu karmasu sthāpayet arthopadhāśuddhān samāhartṛsaṃnidhātṛnicayakarmasu kāmopadhāśuddhān bāhyābhyantaravihārarakṣāsu bhayopadhāśuddhān āsannakāryeṣu rājñaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 13.1]
sarvopadhāśuddhān mantriṇaḥ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 14.1]
sarvatrāśucīn khanidravyahastivanakarmānteṣu upayojayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 15.1]
trivargabhayasaṃśuddhān amātyān sveṣu karmasu | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 16.1]
adhikuryād yathā śaucam ityācāryā vyavasthitāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 16.2]
na tveva kuryād ātmānaṃ devīṃ vā lakṣyam īśvaraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 17.1]
śaucahetor amātyānām etat kauṭilyadarśanam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 17.2]
na dūṣaṇam aduṣṭasya viṣeṇevāmbhasaścaret | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 18.1]
kadāciddhi praduṣṭasya nādhigamyeta bheṣajam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 18.2]
kṛtā ca kaluṣā buddhir upadhābhiścaturvidhā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 19.1]
nāgatvāntaṃ nivarteta sthitā sattvavatāṃ dhṛtau | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 19.2]
tasmād bāhyam adhiṣṭhānaṃ kṛtvā kārye caturvidhe | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 20.1]
śaucāśaucam amātyānāṃ rājā mārgeta sattribhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 10 20.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 11}
upadhābhiḥ śuddhāmātyavargo gūḍhapuruṣān utpādayet kāpaṭikodāsthitagṛhapatikavaidehakatāpasavyañjanān sattritīkṣṇarasadabhikṣukīśca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 1.1]
paramarmajñaḥ pragalbhaśchāttraḥ kāpaṭikaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 2.1]
tam arthamānābhyāṃ protsāhya mantrī brūyāt rājānaṃ māṃ ca pramāṇaṃ kṛtvā yasya yad akuśalaṃ paśyasi tat tadānīm eva pratyādiśa iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 3.1]
pravrajyāpratyavasitaḥ prajñāśaucayukta udāsthitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 4.1]
sa vārttākarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau prabhūtahiraṇyāntevāsī karma kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 5.1]
karmaphalācca sarvapravrajitānāṃ grāsācchādanāvasathān pratividadhyāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 6.1]
vṛttikāmāṃścopajapet etenaiva veṣeṇa rājārthaścaritavyo bhaktavetanakāle copasthātavyam iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 7.1]
sarvapravrajitāśca svaṃ svaṃ vargam evam upajapeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 8.1]
karṣako vṛttikṣīṇaḥ prajñāśaucayukto gṛhapatikavyañjanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 9.1]
sa kṛṣikarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 10.1]
vāṇijako vṛttikṣīṇaḥ prajñāśaucayukto vaidehakavyañjanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 11.1]
sa vaṇikkarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 12.1]
muṇḍo jaṭilo vā vṛttikāmastāpasavyañjanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 13.1]
sa nagarābhyāśe prabhūtamuṇḍajaṭilāntevāsī śākaṃ yavamuṣṭiṃ vā māsadvimāsāntaraṃ prakāśam aśnīyāt gūḍham iṣṭam āhāram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 14.1]
vaidehakāntevāsinaścainaṃ samiddhayogair arcayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 15.1]
śiṣyāścāsyāvedayeyuḥ asau siddhaḥ sāmedhikaḥ iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 16.1]
samedhāśāstibhiścābhigatānām aṅgavidyayā śiṣyasaṃjñābhiśca karmāṇyabhijane avasitānyādiśet alpalābham agnidāhaṃ corabhayaṃ dūṣyavadhaṃ tuṣṭidānaṃ videśapravṛttijñānam idam adya śvo vā bhaviṣyati idaṃ vā rājā kariṣyati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 17.1]
tad asya gūḍhāḥ sattriṇaśca sampādayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 18.1]
sattvaprajñāvākyaśaktisampannānāṃ rājabhāgyam anuvyāharenmantrisaṃyogaṃ ca brūyāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 19.1]
mantrī caiṣāṃ vṛttikarmabhyāṃ viyateta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 20.1]
ye ca kāraṇād abhikruddhāstān arthamānābhyāṃ śamayet akāraṇakruddhāṃstūṣṇīṃ daṇḍena rājadviṣṭakāriṇaśca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 21.1]
pūjitāścārthamānābhyāṃ rājñā rājopajīvinām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 22.1]
jānīyuḥ śaucam ityetāḥ pañcasaṃsthāḥ prakīrtitāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 11 22.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 12}
ye cāpyasaṃbandhino 'vaśyabhartavyāste lakṣaṇam aṅgavidyāṃ jambhakavidyāṃ māyāgatam āśramadharmaṃ nimittam antaracakram ityadhīyānāḥ sattriṇaḥ saṃsargavidyāṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 1.1]
ye janapade śūrāstyaktātmāno hastinaṃ vyālaṃ vā dravyahetoḥ pratiyodhayeyuste tīkṣṇāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 2.1]
ye bandhuṣu niḥsnehāḥ krūrā alasāśca te rasadāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 3.1]
parivrājikā vṛttikāmā daridrā vidhavā pragalbhā brāhmaṇyantaḥpure kṛtasatkārā mahāmātrakulānyabhigacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 4.1]
etayā muṇḍā vṛṣalyo vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 5.1]
tān rājā svaviṣaye mantripurohitasenāpatiyuvarājadauvārikāntarvaṃśikapraśāstṛsamāhartṛsaṃnidhātṛpradeṣṭṛnāyakapauravyāvahārikakārmāntikamantripariṣadadhyakṣadaṇḍadurgāntapālāṭavikeṣu śraddheyadeśaveṣaśilpabhāṣābhijanāpadeśān bhaktitaḥ sāmarthyayogāccāpasarpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 6.1]
teṣāṃ bāhyaṃ cāraṃ chattrabhṛṅgāravyajanapādukāsanayānavāhanopagrāhiṇas tīkṣṇā vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 7.1]
taṃ sattriṇaḥ saṃsthāsvarpayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 8.1]
sūdārālikasnāpakasaṃvāhakāstarakakalpakaprasādhakodakaparicārakā rasadāḥ kubjavāmanakirātamūkabadhirajaḍāndhacchadmāno naṭanartakagāyanavādakavāgjīvanakuśīlavāḥ striyaścābhyantaraṃ cāraṃ vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 9.1]
taṃ bhikṣukyaḥ saṃsthāsvarpayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 10.1]
saṃsthānām antevāsinaḥ saṃjñālipibhiścārasaṃcāraṃ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 11.1]
na cānyonyaṃ saṃsthāste vā vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 12.1]
bhikṣukīpratiṣedhe dvāḥsthaparamparā mātāpitṛvyañjanāḥ śilpakārikāḥ kuśīlavā dāsyo vā gītapāṭhyavādyabhāṇḍagūḍhalekhyasaṃjñābhir vā cāraṃ nirhareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 13.1]
dīrgharogonmādāgnirasavisargeṇa vā gūḍhanirgamanam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 14.1]
trayāṇām ekavākye sampratyayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 15.1]
teṣām abhīkṣṇavinipāte tūṣṇīṃdaṇḍaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 16.1]
kaṇṭakaśodhanoktāścāpasarpāḥ pareṣu kṛtavetanā vaseyur asaṃpātinaścārārtham | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 17.1]
ta ubhayavetanāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 18.1]
gṛhītaputradārāṃśca kuryād ubhayavetanān | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 19.1]
tāṃścāriprahitān vidyāt teṣāṃ śaucaṃ ca tadvidhaiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 19.2]
evaṃ śatrau ca mitre ca madhyame cāvapeccarān | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 20.1]
udāsīne ca teṣāṃ ca tīrtheṣvaṣṭādaśasvapi | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 20.2]
antargṛhacarāsteṣāṃ kubjavāmanapaṇḍakāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 21.1]
śilpavatyaḥ striyo mūkāścitrāśca mlecchajātayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 21.2]
durgeṣu vaṇijaḥ saṃsthā durgānte siddhatāpasāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 22.1]
karṣakodāsthitā rāṣṭre rāṣṭrānte vrajavāsinaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 22.2]
vane vanacarāḥ kāryāḥ śramaṇāṭavikādayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 23.1]
parapravṛttijñānārthāḥ śīghrāścāraparamparāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 23.2]
parasya caite boddhavyāstādṛśair eva tādṛśāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 24.1]
cārasaṃcāriṇaḥ saṃsthā gūḍhāścāgūḍhasaṃjñitāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 24.2]
akṛtyān kṛtyapakṣīyair darśitān kāryahetubhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 25.1]
parāpasarpajñānārthaṃ mukhyān anteṣu vāsayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 12 25.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 13}
kṛtamahāmātrāpasarpaḥ paurajānapadān apasarpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 1.1]
sattriṇo dvaṃdvinas tīrthasabhāpūgajanasamavāyeṣu vivādaṃ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 2.1]
sarvaguṇasampannaścāyaṃ rājā śrūyate na cāsya kaścid guṇo dṛśyate yaḥ paurajānapadān daṇḍakarābhyāṃ pīḍayati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 3.1]
tatra ye 'nupraśaṃseyustān itarastaṃ ca pratiṣedhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 4.1]
mātsyanyāyābhibhūtāḥ prajā manuṃ vaivasvataṃ rājānaṃ cakrire | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 5.1]
dhānyaṣaḍbhāgaṃ paṇyadaśabhāgaṃ hiraṇyaṃ cāsya bhāgadheyaṃ prakalpayāmāsuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 6.1]
tena bhṛtā rājānaḥ prajānāṃ yogakṣemāvahāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 7.1]
teṣāṃ kilbiṣam adaṇḍakarā harantyayogakṣemāvahāśca prajānām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 8.1]
tasmād uñchaṣaḍbhāgam āraṇyakāpi nirvapanti tasyaitad bhāgadheyaṃ yo 'smān gopāyati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 9.1]
indrayamasthānam etad rājānaḥ pratyakṣaheḍaprasādāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 10.1]
tān avamanyamānān daivo 'pi daṇḍaḥ spṛśati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 11.1]
tasmād rājāno nāvamantavyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 12.1]
ityevaṃ kṣudrakān pratiṣedhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 13.1]
kiṃvadantīṃ ca vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 14.1]
ye cāsya dhānyapaśuhiraṇyānyājīvanti tair upakurvanti vyasane 'bhyudaye vā kupitaṃ bandhuṃ rāṣṭraṃ vā vyāvartayanti amitram āṭavikaṃ vā pratiṣedhayanti teṣāṃ muṇḍajaṭilavyañjanāstuṣṭātuṣṭatvaṃ vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 15.1]
tuṣṭān bhūyo 'rthamānābhyāṃ pūjayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 16.1]
atuṣṭāṃstuṣṭihetostyāgena sāmnā ca prasādayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 17.1]
parasparād vā bhedayed enān sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhebhyaśca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 18.1]
tathāpyatuṣyato daṇḍakarasādhanādhikāreṇa janapadavidveṣaṃ grāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 19.1]
vidviṣṭān upāṃśudaṇḍena janapadakopena vā sādhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 20.1]
guptaputradārān ākarakarmānteṣu vā vāsayet pareṣām āspadabhayāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 21.1]
kruddhalubdhabhītamāninastu pareṣāṃ kṛtyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 22.1]
teṣāṃ kārtāntikanaimittikamauhūrtikavyañjanāḥ parasparābhisambandham amitrāṭavikasambandhaṃ vā vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 23.1]
tuṣṭān arthamānābhyāṃ pūjayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 24.1]
atuṣṭān sāmadānabhedadaṇḍaiḥ sādhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 24.2]
evaṃ svaviṣaye kṛtyān akṛtyāṃśca vicakṣaṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 25.1]
paropajāpāt saṃrakṣet pradhānān kṣudrakān api | [ArthaŚ, 1, 13 25.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 14}
kṛtyākṛtyapakṣopagrahaḥ svaviṣaye vyākhyātaḥ paraviṣaye vācyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 1.1]
saṃśrutyārthān vipralabdhaḥ tulyakāriṇoḥ śilpe vopakāre vā vimānitaḥ vallabhāvaruddhaḥ samāhūya parājitaḥ pravāsopataptaḥ kṛtvā vyayam alabdhakāryaḥ svadharmād dāyādyād voparuddhaḥ mānādhikārābhyāṃ bhraṣṭaḥ kulyair antarhitaḥ prasabhābhimṛṣṭastrīkaḥ kārābhinyastaḥ paroktadaṇḍitaḥ mithyācāravāritaḥ sarvasvam āhāritaḥ bandhanaparikliṣṭaḥ pravāsitabandhuḥ iti kruddhavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 2.1]
svayam upahataḥ viprakṛtaḥ pāpakarmābhikhyātaḥ tulyadoṣadaṇḍenodvignaḥ paryāttabhūmiḥ daṇḍenopanataḥ sarvādhikaraṇasthaḥ sahasopacitārthaḥ tatkulīno vāśaṃsuḥ pradviṣṭo rājñā rājadveṣī ca iti bhītavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 3.1]
parikṣīṇaḥ anyāttasvaḥ kadaryaḥ vyasanī atyāhitavyavahāraśca iti lubdhavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 4.1]
ātmasaṃbhāvitaḥ mānakāmaḥ śatrupūjāmarṣitaḥ nīcair upahitaḥ tīkṣṇaḥ sāhasikaḥ bhogenāsaṃtuṣṭaḥ iti mānivargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 5.1]
teṣāṃ muṇḍajaṭilavyañjanair yo yadbhaktiḥ kṛtyapakṣīyastaṃ tenopajāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 6.1]
yathā madāndho hastī mattenādhiṣṭhito yad yad āsādayati tat sarvaṃ pramṛdnāti evam ayam aśāstracakṣur andho rājā paurajānapadavadhāyābhyutthitaḥ śakyam asya pratihastiprotsāhanenāpakartum amarṣaḥ kriyatām iti kruddhavargam upajāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 7.1]
yathā līnaḥ sarpo yasmād bhayaṃ paśyati tatra viṣam utsṛjati evam ayaṃ rājā jātadoṣāśaṅkastvayi purā krodhaviṣam utsṛjati anyatra gamyatām iti bhītavargam upajāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 8.1]
yathā śvagaṇināṃ dhenuḥ śvabhyo duhyate na brāhmaṇebhyaḥ evam ayaṃ rājā sattvaprajñāvākyaśaktihīnebhyo duhyate nātmaguṇasampannebhyaḥ asau rājā puruṣaviśeṣajñaḥ tatra gamyatām iti lubdhavargam upajāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 9.1]
yathā caṇḍālodapānaścaṇḍālānām evopabhogyo nānyeṣām evam ayaṃ rājā nīco nīcānām evopabhogyo na tvadvidhānām āryāṇām asau rājā puruṣaviśeṣajñaḥ tatra gamyatām iti mānivargam upajāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 10.1]
tatheti pratipannāṃstān saṃhitān paṇakarmaṇā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 11.1]
yojayeta yathāśakti sāpasarpān svakarmasu | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 11.2]
labheta sāmadānābhyāṃ kṛtyāṃśca parabhūmiṣu | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 12.1]
akṛtyān bhedadaṇḍābhyāṃ paradoṣāṃśca darśayan | [ArthaŚ, 1, 14 12.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 15}
kṛtasvapakṣaparapakṣopagrahaḥ kāryārambhāṃścintayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 1.1]
mantrapūrvāḥ sarvārambhāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 2.1]
taduddeśaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ kathānām aniḥśrāvī pakṣibhir apyanālokyaḥ syāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 3.1]
śrūyate hi śukasārikābhir mantro bhinnaḥ śvabhir apyanyaiśca tiryagyonibhir iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 3.2]
tasmān mantroddeśam anāyukto nopagacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 4.1]
ucchidyeta mantrabhedī | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 5.1]
mantrabhedo hi dūtāmātyasvāminām iṅgitākārābhyām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 6.1]
iṅgitam anyathāvṛttiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 7.1]
ākṛtigrahaṇam ākāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 8.1]
tasya saṃvaraṇam āyuktapuruṣarakṣaṇam ā kāryakālād iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 9.1]
teṣāṃ hi pramādamadasuptapralāpāḥ kāmādir utsekaḥ pracchanno 'vamato vā mantraṃ bhinatti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 10.1]
tasmād rakṣen mantram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 11.1]
mantrabhedo hyayogakṣemakaro rājñastadāyuktapuruṣāṇāṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 12.1]
tasmād guhyam eko mantrayeta iti bhāradvājaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 13.1]
mantriṇām api hi mantriṇo bhavanti teṣām apyanye | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 14.1]
saiṣā mantriparamparā mantraṃ bhinatti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 15.1]
tasmān nāsya pare vidyuḥ karma kiṃciccikīrṣitam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 16.1]
ārabdhārastu jānīyur ārabdhaṃ kṛtam eva vā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 16.2]
naikasya mantrasiddhir asti iti viśālākṣaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 17.1]
pratyakṣaparokṣānumeyā hi rājavṛttiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 18.1]
anupalabdhasya jñānam upalabdhasya niścitabalādhānam arthadvaidhasya saṃśayacchedanam ekadeśadṛṣṭasya śeṣopalabdhir iti mantrisādhyam etat | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 19.1]
tasmād buddhivṛddhaiḥ sārdham adhyāsīta mantram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 20.1]
na kaṃcid avamanyeta sarvasya śṛṇuyān matam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 21.1]
bālasyāpyarthavadvākyam upayuñjīta paṇḍitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 21.2]
etan mantrajñānam naitan mantrarakṣaṇam iti pārāśarāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 22.1]
yad asya kāryam abhipretaṃ tatpratirūpakaṃ mantriṇaḥ pṛcchet kāryam idam evam āsīt evaṃ vā yadi bhavet tat kathaṃ kartavyam iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 23.1]
te yathā brūyustat kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 24.1]
evaṃ mantropalabdhiḥ saṃvṛtiśca bhavati iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 25.1]
neti piśunaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 26.1]
mantriṇo hi vyavahitam arthaṃ vṛttam avṛttaṃ vā pṛṣṭā anādareṇa bruvanti prakāśayanti vā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 27.1]
sa doṣaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 28.1]
tasmāt karmasu ye yeṣvabhipretāstaiḥ saha mantrayeta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 29.1]
tair mantrayamāṇo hi mantrasiddhiṃ guptiṃ ca labhate iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 30.1]
neti kauṭilyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 31.1]
anavasthā hyeṣā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 32.1]
mantribhistribhiścaturbhir vā saha mantrayeta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 33.1]
mantrayamāṇo hyekenārthakṛcchreṣu niścayaṃ nādhigacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 34.1]
ekaśca mantrī yatheṣṭam anavagrahaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 15 35.1]

{ArthaŚ, 1, 18}

pāragrāmikaṃ vā yogam ātiṣṭhet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 18 10.1]

ityaparuddhavṛttam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 18 12.2]

upasthitaṃ ca rājyena madūrdhvam iti sāntvayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 18 15.1]

saptame mantram adhyāsīta gūḍhapuruṣāṃśca preṣayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 21.1]
aṣṭame ṛtvigācāryapurohitasvastyayanāni pratigṛhṇīyāt cikitsakamāhānasikamauhūrtikāṃśca paśyet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 22.1]
savatsāṃ dhenuṃ vṛṣabhaṃ ca pradakṣiṇīkṛtyopasthānaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 23.1]
ātmabalānukūlyena vā niśāharbhāgān pravibhajya kāryāṇi seveta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 24.1]
upasthānagataḥ kāryārthinām advārāsaṅgaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 25.1]
durdarśo hi rājā kāryākāryaviparyāsam āsannaiḥ kāryate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 26.1]
tena prakṛtikopam arivaśaṃ vā gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 27.1]
tasmād devatāśramapāṣaṇḍaśrotriyapaśupuṇyasthānānāṃ bālavṛddhavyādhitavyasanyanāthānāṃ strīṇāṃ ca krameṇa kāryāṇi paśyet kāryagauravād ātyayikavaśena vā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 28.1]
sarvam ātyayikaṃ kāryaṃ śṛṇuyān nātipātayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 29.1]
kṛcchrasādhyam atikrāntam asādhyaṃ vāpi jāyate | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 29.2]
agnyagāragataḥ kāryaṃ paśyed vaidyatapasvinām | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 30.1]
purohitācāryasakhaḥ pratyutthāyābhivādya ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 30.2]
tapasvināṃ tu kāryāṇi traividyaiḥ saha kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 31.1]
māyāyogavidāṃ caiva na svayaṃ kopakāraṇāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 31.2]
rājño hi vratam utthānaṃ yajñaḥ kāryānuśāsanam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 32.1]
dakṣiṇā vṛttisāmyaṃ tu dīkṣā tasyābhiṣecanam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 32.2]
prajāsukhe sukhaṃ rājñaḥ prajānāṃ ca hite hitam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 33.1]
nātmapriyaṃ hitaṃ rājñaḥ prajānāṃ tu priyaṃ hitam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 33.2]
tasmān nityotthito rājā kuryād arthānuśāsanam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 34.1]
arthasya mūlam utthānam anarthasya viparyayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 34.2]
anutthāne dhruvo nāśaḥ prāptasyānāgatasya ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 35.1]
prāpyate phalam utthānāllabhate cārthasampadam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 19 35.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 20}
vāstukapraśaste deśe saprākāraparikhādvāram anekakakṣyāparigatam antaḥpuraṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 1.1]
kośagṛhavidhānena madhye vāsagṛham gūḍhabhittisaṃcāraṃ mohanagṛhaṃ tanmadhye vā vāsagṛham bhūmigṛhaṃ vāsannacaityakāṣṭhadevatāpidhānadvāram anekasuruṅgāsaṃcāraṃ tasyopari prāsādaṃ gūḍhabhittisopānaṃ suṣirastambhapraveśāpasāraṃ vā vāsagṛhaṃ yantrabaddhatalāvapātaṃ kārayet āpatpratīkārārtham āpadi vā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 2.1]
ato 'nyathā vā vikalpayet sahādhyāyibhayāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 3.1]
mānuṣeṇāgninā trir apasavyaṃ parigatam antaḥpuram agnir anyo na dahati na cātrānyo 'gnir jvalati vaidyutena bhasmanā mṛtsaṃyuktena karakavāriṇāvaliptaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 4.1]
jīvantīśvetāmuṣkakapuṣpavandākābhir akṣīve jātasyāśvatthasya pratānena guptaṃ sarpā viṣāṇi vā na prabhavanti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 5.1]
mayūranakulapṛṣatotsargaḥ sarpān bhakṣayati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 6.1]
śukaḥ sārikā bhṛṅgarājo vā sarpaviṣaśaṅkāyāṃ krośati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 7.1]
krauñco viṣābhyāśe mādyati glāyati jīvaṃjīvakaḥ mriyate mattakokilaḥ cakorasyākṣiṇī virajyete | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 8.1]
ityevam agniviṣasarpebhyaḥ pratikurvīta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 9.1]
pṛṣṭhataḥ kakṣyāvibhāge strīniveśo garbhavyādhisaṃsthā vṛkṣodakasthānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 10.1]
bahiḥ kanyākumārapuram | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 11.1]
purastād alaṅkārabhūmir mantrabhūmir upasthānaṃ kumārādhyakṣasthānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 12.1]
kakṣyāntareṣvantarvaṃśikasainyaṃ tiṣṭhet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 13.1]
antargṛhagataḥ sthavirastrīpariśuddhāṃ devīṃ paśyet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 14.1]
devīgṛhe līno hi bhrātā bhadrasenaṃ jaghāna mātuḥ śayyāntargataśca putraḥ kārūṣam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 15.1]
lājān madhuneti viṣeṇa paryasya devī kāśirājam viṣadigdhena nūpureṇa vairantyam mekhalāmaṇinā sauvīram jālūtham ādarśena veṇyāṃ gūḍhaṃ śastraṃ kṛtvā devī vidūrathaṃ jaghāna | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 16.1]
tasmād etānyāspadāni pariharet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 17.1]
muṇḍajaṭilakuhakapratisaṃsargaṃ bāhyābhiśca dāsībhiḥ pratiṣedhayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 18.1]
na caināḥ kulyāḥ paśyeyuḥ anyatra garbhavyādhisaṃsthābhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 19.1]
rūpājīvāḥ snānapragharṣaśuddhaśarīrāḥ parivartitavastrālaṃkārāḥ paśyeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 20.1]
aśītikāḥ puruṣāḥ pañcāśatkāḥ striyo vā mātāpitṛvyañjanāḥ sthaviravarṣadharābhyāgārikāścāvarodhānāṃ śaucāśaucaṃ vidyuḥ sthāpayeyuśca svāmihite | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 21.1]
svabhūmau ca vaset sarvaḥ parabhūmau na saṃcaret | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 22.1]
na ca bāhyena saṃsargaṃ kaścid ābhyantaro vrajet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 22.2]
sarvaṃ cāvekṣitaṃ dravyaṃ nibaddhāgamanirgamam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 23.1]
nirgacched abhigacched vā mudrāsaṃkrāntabhūmikam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 20 23.2]
{ArthaŚ, 1, 21}
śayanād utthitaḥ strīgaṇair dhanvibhiḥ parigṛhyate dvitīyasyāṃ kakṣyāyāṃ kaṃcukoṣṇīṣibhir varṣadharābhyāgārikaiḥ tṛtīyasyāṃ kubjavāmanakirātaiḥ caturthyāṃ mantribhiḥ sambandhibhir dauvārikaiśca prāsapāṇibhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 1.1]
pitṛpaitāmahaṃ sambandhānubaddhaṃ śikṣitam anuraktaṃ kṛtakarmāṇaṃ ca janam āsannaṃ kurvīta nānyatodeśīyam akṛtārthamānaṃ svadeśīyaṃ vāpyapakṛtyopagṛhītam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 2.1]
antarvaṃśikasainyaṃ rājānam antaḥpuraṃ ca rakṣet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 3.1]
gupte deśe māhānasikaḥ sarvam āsvādabāhulyena karma kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 4.1]
tad rājā tathaiva pratibhuñjīta pūrvam agnaye vayobhyaśca baliṃ kṛtvā | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 5.1]
agner jvālādhūmanīlatā śabdasphoṭanaṃ ca viṣayuktasya vayasāṃ vipattiśca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 6.1]
annasya ūṣmā mayūragrīvābhaḥ śaityam āśu kliṣṭasyeva vaivarṇyaṃ saudakatvam aklinnatvaṃ ca vyañjanānām āśu śuṣkatvaṃ ca kvāthadhyāmaphenapaṭalavicchinnabhāvo gandhasparśarasavadhaśca draveṣu hīnātiriktacchāyādarśanaṃ phenapaṭalasīmantordhvarājīdarśanaṃ ca rasasya madhye nīlā rājī payasastāmrā madyatoyayoḥ kālī dadhnaḥ śyāmā madhunaḥ śvetā dravyāṇām ārdrāṇām āśu pramlānatvam utpakvabhāvaḥ kvāthanīlaśyāvatā ca śuṣkāṇām āśu śātanaṃ vaivarṇyaṃ ca kaṭhinānāṃ mṛdutvaṃ mṛdūnāṃ ca kaṭhinatvam tadabhyāśe kṣudrasattvavadhaśca āstaraṇaprāvaraṇānāṃ dhyāmamaṇḍalatā tanturomapakṣmaśātanaṃ ca lohamaṇimayānāṃ paṅkamalopadehatā sneharāgagauravaprabhāvavarṇasparśavadhaśca iti viṣayuktasya liṅgāni | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 7.1]
viṣapradasya tu śuṣkaśyāvavaktratā vāksaṅgaḥ svedo vijṛmbhaṇaṃ cātimātraṃ vepathuḥ praskhalanaṃ vākyaviprekṣaṇam āvegaḥ karmaṇi svabhūmau cānavasthānam iti | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 8.1]
tasmād asya jāṅgulīvido bhiṣajaścāsannāḥ syuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 9.1]
bhiṣagbhaiṣajyāgārād āsvādaviśuddham auṣadhaṃ gṛhītvā pācakapeṣakābhyām ātmanā ca pratisvādya rājñe prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 10.1]
pānaṃ pānīyaṃ cauṣadhena vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 11.1]
kalpakaprasādhakāḥ snānaśuddhavastrahastāḥ samudram upakaraṇam antarvaṃśikahastād ādāya paricareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 12.1]
snāpakasaṃvāhakāstarakarajakamālākārakarma dāsyaḥ prasiddhaśaucāḥ kuryuḥ tābhir adhiṣṭhitā vā śilpinaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 13.1]
ātmacakṣuṣi niveśya vastramālyaṃ dadyuḥ snānānulepanapragharṣacūrṇavāsasnānīyāni ca svavakṣobāhuṣu ca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 14.1]
etena parasmād āgatakaṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 15.1]
kuśīlavāḥ śastrāgnirasakrīḍāvarjaṃ narmayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 16.1]
ātodyāni caiṣām antastiṣṭheyuḥ aśvarathadvipālaṃkārāśca | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 17.1]
āptapuruṣādhiṣṭhitaṃ yānavāhanam ārohet nāvaṃ cāptanāvikādhiṣṭhitam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 18.1]
anyanaupratibaddhāṃ vātavegavaśāṃ ca nopeyāt | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 19.1]
udakānte sainyam āsīta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 20.1]
matsyagrāhaviśuddham udakam avagāheta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 21.1]
vyālagrāhaviśuddham udyānaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 22.1]
lubdhakaśvagaṇibhir apāstastenavyālaparābādhabhayaṃ calalakṣyaparicayārthaṃ mṛgāraṇyaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 23.1]
āptaśastragrāhādhiṣṭhitaḥ siddhatāpasaṃ paśyenmantripariṣadā saha sāmantadūtam | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 24.1]
saṃnaddho 'śvaṃ hastinaṃ vārūḍhaḥ saṃnaddham anīkaṃ paśyet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 25.1]
niryāṇe 'bhiyāne ca rājamārgam ubhayataḥ kṛtārakṣaṃ śastribhir daṇḍibhiścāpāstaśastrahastapravrajitavyaṅgaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 26.1]
na puruṣasambādham avagāheta | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 27.1]
yātrāsamājotsavapravahaṇāni ca daśavargikādhiṣṭhitāni gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 28.1]
yathā ca yogapuruṣair anyān rājādhitiṣṭhati | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 29.1]
tathāyam anyābādhebhyo rakṣed ātmānam ātmavān | [ArthaŚ, 1, 21 29.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 1}
bhūtapūrvam abhūtapūrvaṃ vā janapadaṃ paradeśāpavāhanena svadeśābhiṣyandavamanena vā niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 1.1]
śūdrakarṣakaprāyaṃ kulaśatāvaraṃ pañcakulaśataparaṃ grāmaṃ krośadvikrośasīmānam anyonyārakṣaṃ niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 2.1]
nadīśailavanabhṛṣṭidarīsetubandhaśamīśālmalīkṣīravṛkṣān anteṣu sīmnāṃ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 3.1]
aṣṭaśatagrāmyā madhye sthānīyam catuḥśatagrāmyā droṇamukham dviśatagrāmyāḥ kārvaṭikam daśagrāmīsaṃgraheṇa saṃgrahaṃ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 4.1]
anteṣvantapāladurgāṇi janapadadvārāṇyantapālādhiṣṭhitāni sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 5.1]
teṣām antarāṇi vāgurikaśabarapulindacaṇḍālāraṇyacarā rakṣeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 6.1]
ṛtvigācāryapurohitaśrotriyebhyo brahmadeyāny adaṇḍakarāṇy abhirūpadāyādakāni prayacchet adhyakṣasaṃkhyāyakādibhyo gopasthānikānīkasthacikitsakāśvadamakajaṅghākārikebhyaśca vikrayādhānavarjāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 7.1]
karadebhyaḥ kṛtakṣetrāṇyaikapuruṣikāṇi prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 8.1]
akṛtāni kartṛbhyo nādeyāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 9.1]
akṛṣatām ācchidyānyebhyaḥ prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 10.1]
grāmabhṛtakavaidehakā vā kṛṣeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 11.1]
akṛṣanto vāvahīnaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 12.1]
dhānyapaśuhiraṇyaiścaitān anugṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 13.1]
tānyanu sukhena dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 14.1]
anugrahaparihārau caitebhyaḥ kośavṛddhikarau dadyāt kośopaghātakau varjayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 15.1]
alpakośo hi rājā paurajānapadān eva grasate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 16.1]
niveśasamakālaṃ yathāgatakaṃ vā parihāraṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 17.1]
nivṛttaparihārān pitevānugṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 18.1]
ākarakarmāntadravyahastivanavrajavaṇikpathapracārān vāristhalapathapaṇyapattanāni ca niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 19.1]
sahodakam āhāryodakaṃ vā setuṃ bandhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 20.1]
anyeṣāṃ vā badhnatāṃ bhūmimārgavṛkṣopakaraṇānugrahaṃ kuryāt puṇyasthānārāmāṇāṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 21.1]
sambhūya setubandhād apakrāmataḥ karmakarabalīvardāḥ karma kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 22.1]
vyayakarmaṇi ca bhāgī syāt na cāṃśaṃ labheta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 23.1]
matsyaplavaharitapaṇyānāṃ setuṣu rājā svāmyaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 24.1]
dāsāhitakabandhūn aśṛṇvato rājā vinayaṃ grāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 25.1]
bālavṛddhavyasanyanāthāṃśca rājā bibhṛyāt striyam aprajātāṃ prajātāyāśca putrān | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 26.1]
bāladravyaṃ grāmavṛddhā vardhayeyur ā vyavahāraprāpaṇāt devadravyaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 27.1]
apatyadāraṃ mātāpitarau bhrātṝn aprāptavyavahārān bhaginīḥ kanyā vidhavāścābibhrataḥ śaktimato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ anyatra patitebhyaḥ anyatra mātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 28.1]
putradāram apratividhāya pravrajataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ striyaṃ ca pravrājayataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 29.1]
luptavyāyāmaḥ pravrajed āpṛcchya dharmasthān | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 30.1]
anyathā niyamyeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 31.1]
vānaprasthād anyaḥ pravrajitabhāvaḥ sajātād anyaḥ saṃghaḥ sāmutthāyikād anyaḥ samayānubandho vā nāsya janapadam upaniviśeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 32.1]
na ca tatrārāmā vihārārthā vā śālāḥ syuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 33.1]
naṭanartakagāyanavādakavāgjīvanakuśīlavā na karmavighnaṃ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 34.1]
nirāśrayatvād grāmāṇāṃ kṣetrābhiratatvācca puruṣāṇāṃ kośaviṣṭidravyadhānyarasavṛddhir bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 35.1]
paracakrāṭavīgrastaṃ vyādhidurbhikṣapīḍitam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 36.1]
deśaṃ parihared rājā vyayakrīḍāśca vārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 36.2]
daṇḍaviṣṭikarābādhai rakṣed upahatāṃ kṛṣim | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 37.1]
stenavyālaviṣagrāhair vyādhibhiśca paśuvrajān | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 37.2]
vallabhaiḥ kārmikaiḥ stenair antapālaiśca pīḍitam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 38.1]
śodhayet paśusaṃghaiśca kṣīyamāṇaṃ vaṇikpatham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 38.2]
evaṃ dravyadvipavanaṃ setubandham athākarān | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 39.1]
rakṣet pūrvakṛtān rājā navāṃścābhipravartayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 1 39.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 2}
akṛṣyāyāṃ bhūmau paśubhyo vivītāni prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 1.1]
pradiṣṭābhayasthāvarajaṅgamāni ca brahmasomāraṇyāni tapasvibhyo gorutaparāṇi prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 2.1]
tāvanmātram ekadvāraṃ khātaguptaṃ svāduphalagulmaguccham akaṇṭakidrumam uttānatoyāśayaṃ dāntamṛgacatuṣpadaṃ bhagnanakhadaṃṣṭravyālaṃ mārgayukahastihastinīkalabhaṃ mṛgavanaṃ vihārārthaṃ rājñaḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 3.1]
sarvātithimṛgaṃ pratyante cānyanmṛgavanaṃ bhūmivaśena vā niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 4.1]
kupyapradiṣṭānāṃ ca dravyāṇām ekaikaśo vanāni niveśayet dravyavanakarmāntān aṭavīśca dravyavanāpāśrayāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 5.1]
pratyante hastivanam aṭavyārakṣaṃ niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 6.1]
nāgavanādhyakṣaḥ pārvataṃ nādeyaṃ sārasamānūpaṃ ca nāgavanaṃ viditaparyantapraveśaniṣkāsaṃ nāgavanapālaiḥ pālayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 7.1]
hastighātinaṃ hanyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 8.1]
dantayugaṃ svayaṃmṛtasyāharataḥ sapādacatuṣpaṇo lābhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 9.1]
nāgavanapālā hastipakapādapāśikasaumikavanacarakapārikarmikasakhā hastimūtrapurīṣacchannagandhā bhallātakīśākhāpracchannāḥ pañcabhiḥ saptabhir vā hastibandhakībhiḥ saha carantaḥ śayyāsthānapadyāleṇḍakūlaghātoddeśena hastikulaparyagraṃ vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 10.1]
yūthacaram ekacaraṃ niryūthaṃ yūthapatiṃ hastinaṃ vyālaṃ mattaṃ potaṃ bandhamuktaṃ ca nibandhena vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 11.1]
anīkasthapramāṇaiḥ praśastavyañjanācārān hastino gṛhṇīyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 12.1]
hastipradhānaṃ vijayo rājñaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 2 13.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 3}
caturdiśam janapada ante sāmparāyikam daiva kṛtam durgam kārayet antar dvīpam sthalam _ nimna avaruddham audakam prāstaram guhām _ pārvatam nirudaka stambam iriṇam _ dhānvanam khañjana udakam stamba gahanam _ vana durgam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463964_1]
teṣām nadī parvata durgam janapada ārakṣa sthānam dhānvana vana durgam aṭavī sthānam āpadi apasāraḥ _ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463965_1]
janapada madhye samudaya sthānam sthānīyam niveśayet vāstuka praśaste deśe nadī saṃgame hradasya a viśoṣasya aṅke sarasaḥ taṭākasya _ vṛttam dīrgham caturaśram _ vāstu vaśena _ pradakṣiṇa udakam paṇya puṭabhedanam aṃsa patha vāri pathābhyām upetam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463966_1]
tasya parikhāḥ tisraḥ daṇḍa antarāḥ kārayet caturdaśa dvādaśa daśa iti daṇḍān vistīrṇāḥ vistārāt avagāḍhāḥ pāda ūnam ardham _ tri bhāga mūlāḥ mūla caturaśrāḥ _ pāṣāṇa upahitāḥ pāṣāṇa iṣṭakā baddha pārśvāḥ _ toya āntikāḥ āgantu toya pūrṇāḥ _ sa parivāhāḥ padma grāhavatīḥ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463967_1]
catur daṇḍa apakṛṣṭam parikhāyāḥ ṣaṣ daṇḍa ucchritam avaruddham tad dviguṇa viṣkambham khātāt vapram kārayet ūrdhva cayam mañca pṛṣṭham kumbhakukṣikam _ hastibhiḥ gobhiḥ ca kṣuṇṇam kaṇṭaki gulma viṣa vallī pratānavantam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463968_1]
pāṃsu śeṣeṇa vāstu chidram rāja bhavanam _ pūrayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463969_1]
vaprasya upari prākāram viṣkambha dviguṇa utsedham aiṣṭakam dvādaśa hastāt ūrdhvam ojam yugmam _ ā caturviṃśati hastāt iti kārayet ratha caryā saṃcāram tāla mūlam murajakaiḥ kapiśīrṣakaiḥ ca ācita agram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463970_1]
pṛthu śilā saṃhatam _ śailam kārayet na tu eva kāṣṭha mayam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463971_1]
agniḥ avahitaḥ hi tasmin vasati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463972_1]
viṣkambha caturaśram aṭṭālakam utsedha sama avakṣepa sopānam kārayet triṃśat daṇḍa antaram ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463973_1]
dvayoḥ aṭṭālakayoḥ madhye sa harmya dvi talām adhyardha āyāmām pratolīm kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463974_1]
aṭṭālaka pratolī madhye tri dhānuṣka adhiṣṭhānam sa apidhāna chidra phalaka saṃhatam indrakośam kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463975_1]
antareṣu dvi hasta viṣkambham pārśve caturguṇa āyāmam devapatham kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463976_1]
daṇḍa antarāḥ dvi daṇḍa antarāḥ _ caryāḥ kārayet a grāhye deśe pradhāvanikām niṣkira dvāram ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463977_1]
bahis jānu bhañjanī śūla prakara kūpa kūṭa avapāta kaṇṭaka pratisara ahipṛṣṭha tālapattra śṛṅgāṭaka śvadaṃṣṭrā argala upaskandana pāduka ambarīṣa udapānakaiḥ praticchannam channa patham kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463978_1]
prākāram ubhayatas meṇḍhakam adhyardha daṇḍam kṛtvā pratolī ṣaṣ tulā antaram dvāram niveśayet pañca daṇḍāt eka uttaram ā aṣṭa daṇḍāt iti caturaśram ṣaṣ bhāgam āyāmāt adhikam aṣṭa bhāgam _ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463979_1]
pañcadaśa hastāt eka uttaram ā aṣṭādaśa hastāt iti tala utsedhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463980_1]
stambhasya parikṣepaḥ ṣaṣ āyāmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463981_1]
dviguṇaḥ nikhātaḥ cūlikāyāḥ catur bhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463981_2]
ādi talasya pañca bhāgāḥ śālāḥ vāpī sīmā gṛham ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463982_1]
daśa bhāgikau dvau pratimañcau antaram āṇi harmyam ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463983_1]
samucchrayāt ardha tale sthūṇā bandhaḥ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463984_1]
ardha vāstukam uttama āgāram tri bhāga antaram _ iṣṭakā avabaddha pārśvam vāmatas pradakṣiṇa sopānam gūḍha bhitti sopānam itaratas | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463985_1]
dvi hastam toraṇa śiraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463986_1]
tri pañca bhāgikau dvau kapāṭa yogau | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463987_1]
dvau parighau | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463988_1]
aratniḥ indrakīlaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463989_1]
pañca hastam āṇi dvāram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463990_1]
catvāraḥ hasti parighāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463991_1]
niveśa ardham hastinakham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463992_1]
mukha samaḥ saṃkramaḥ saṃhāryaḥ bhūmi mayaḥ _ nirudake | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463993_1]
prākāra samam mukham avasthāpya tri bhāga godhā mukham gopuram kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463994_1]
prākāra madhye vāpīm kṛtvā puṣkariṇī dvāram catur śālam adhyardha antaram kumārīpuram muṇḍa harmya dvi talam muṇḍaka dvāram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463995_1]
bhūmi dravya vaśena _ niveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463995_2]
tri bhāga adhika āyāmāḥ bhāṇḍa vāhinīḥ kulyāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463996_1]
tāsu pāṣāṇa kuddālāḥ kuṭhārī kāṇḍa kalpanāḥ muṣuṇḍhī mudgarāḥ daṇḍāḥ cakrayantra śataghnyaḥ kāryāḥ kārmārikāḥ śūlāḥ vedhana agrāḥ ca veṇavaḥ uṣṭragrīvyaḥ agni saṃyogāḥ kupya kalpe ca yaḥ vidhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 3 463999_1]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 4}
trayaḥ prācīnā rājamārgāstraya udīcīnā iti vāstuvibhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 1.1]
sa dvādaśadvāro yuktodakabhramacchannapathaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 2.1]
caturdaṇḍāntarā rathyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 3.1]
rājamārgadroṇamukhasthānīyarāṣṭravivītapathāḥ samyānīyavyūhaśmaśānagrāmapathāś cāṣṭadaṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 4.1]
caturdaṇḍaḥ setuvanapathaḥ dvidaṇḍo hastikṣetrapathaḥ pañcāratnayo rathapathaḥ catvāraḥ paśupathaḥ dvau kṣudrapaśumanuṣyapathaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 5.1]
pravīre vāstuni rājaniveśaś cāturvarṇyasamājīve | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 6.1]
vāstuhṛdayād uttare navabhāge yathoktavidhānam antaḥpuraṃ prāṅmukham udaṅmukhaṃ vā kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 7.1]
tasya pūrvottaraṃ bhāgam ācāryapurohitejyātoyasthānaṃ mantriṇaścāvaseyuḥ pūrvadakṣiṇaṃ bhāgam mahānasaṃ hastiśālā koṣṭhāgāraṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 8.1]
tataḥ paraṃ gandhamālyarasapaṇyāḥ prasādhanakāravaḥ kṣatriyāśca pūrvāṃ diśam adhivaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 9.1]
dakṣiṇapūrvaṃ bhāgaṃ bhāṇḍāgāram akṣapaṭalaṃ karmaniṣadyāśca dakṣiṇapaścimaṃ bhāgaṃ kupyagṛham āyudhāgāraṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 10.1]
tataḥ paraṃ nagaradhānyavyāvahārikakārmāntikabalādhyakṣāḥ pakvānnasurāmāṃsapaṇyā rūpājīvāstālāvacarā vaiśyāśca dakṣiṇāṃ diśam adhivaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 11.1]
paścimadakṣiṇaṃ bhāgaṃ kharoṣṭraguptisthānaṃ karmagṛhaṃ ca paścimottaraṃ bhāgaṃ yānarathaśālāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 12.1]

tataḥ paraṃ nagararājadevatālohamaṇikāravo brāhmaṇāścottarāṃ diśam adhivaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 15.1]
vāstucchidrānuśāleṣu śreṇīprapaṇinikāyā āvaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 16.1]
aparājitāpratihatajayantavaijayantakoṣṭhān śivavaiśravaṇāśviśrīmadirāgṛhāṇi ca puramadhye kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 17.1]
yathoddeśaṃ vāstudevatāḥ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 18.1]
brāhmaindrayāmyasaināpatyāni dvārāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 19.1]
bahiḥ parikhāyā dhanuḥśatāpakṛṣṭāś caityapuṇyasthānavanasetubandhāḥ kāryāḥ yathādiśaṃ ca digdevatāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 20.1]
uttaraḥ pūrvo vā śmaśānabhāgo varṇottamānām dakṣiṇena śmaśānaṃ varṇāvarāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 21.1]
tasyātikrame pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 22.1]
pāṣaṇḍacaṇḍālānāṃ śmaśānānte vāsaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 23.1]

daśakulīvāṭaṃ kūpasthānam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 26.1]
sarvasnehadhānyakṣāralavaṇagandhabhaiṣajyaśuṣkaśākayavasavallūratṛṇakāṣṭhalohacarmāṅgārasnāyuviṣaviṣāṇaveṇuvalkalasāradārupraharaṇāvaraṇāśmanicayān anekavarṣopabhogasahān kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 27.1]
navenānavaṃ śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 4 28.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 5}
saṃnidhātā kośagṛhaṃ paṇyagṛhaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ kupyagṛham āyudhāgāraṃ bandhanāgāraṃ ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 1.1]
caturaśrāṃ vāpīm anudakopasnehāṃ khānayitvā pṛthuśilābhir ubhayataḥ pārśvaṃ mūlaṃ ca pracitya sāradārupañjaraṃ bhūmisamaṃ tritalam anekavidhānaṃ kuṭṭimadeśasthānatalam ekadvāraṃ yantrayuktasopānaṃ bhūmigṛhaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 2.1]
tasyoparyubhayatoniṣedhaṃ sapragrīvam aiṣṭakaṃ bhāṇḍavāhinīparikṣiptaṃ kośagṛhaṃ kārayet prāsādaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 3.1]
janapadānte dhruvanidhim āpadartham abhityaktaiḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 4.1]
pakveṣṭakāstambhaṃ catuḥśālam ekadvāram anekasthānatalaṃ vivṛtastambhāpasāram ubhayataḥ paṇyagṛhaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ ca dīrghabahuśālaṃ kakṣyāvṛtakuḍyam antaḥ kupyagṛham tad eva bhūmigṛhayuktam āyudhāgāraṃ pṛthagdharmasthīyaṃ mahāmātrīyaṃ vibhaktastrīpuruṣasthānam apasārataḥ suguptakakṣyaṃ bandhanāgāraṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 5.1]
sarveṣāṃ śālāḥ khātodapānavacca snānagṛhāgniviṣatrāṇamārjāranakulārakṣāsvadaivatapūjanayuktāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 6.1]
koṣṭhāgāre varṣamānam aratnimukhaṃ kuṇḍaṃ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 7.1]
tajjātakaraṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ purāṇaṃ navaṃ ca ratnaṃ sāraṃ phalgu kupyaṃ vā pratigṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 8.1]
tatra ratnopadhāv uttamo daṇḍaḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca sāropadhau madhyamaḥ phalgukupyopadhau tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 9.1]
rūpadarśakaviśuddhaṃ hiraṇyaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 10.1]
aśuddhaṃ chedayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 11.1]
āhartuḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 12.1]
śuddhaṃ pūrṇam abhinavaṃ ca dhānyaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 13.1]
viparyaye mūlyadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 14.1]
tena paṇyaṃ kupyam āyudhaṃ ca vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 15.1]
sarvādhikaraṇeṣu yuktopayuktatatpuruṣāṇāṃ paṇādicatuṣpaṇaparamāpahāreṣu pūrvamadhyamottamavadhā daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 16.1]
kośādhiṣṭhitasya kośāvacchede ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 17.1]
tadvaiyāvṛtyakarāṇām ardhadaṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 18.1]
paribhāṣaṇam avijñāte | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 19.1]
corāṇām abhipradharṣaṇe citro ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 20.1]

yathā pṛṣṭo na sajjeta vyaye śeṣe ca saṃcaye | [ArthaŚ, 2, 5 22.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 6}
samāhartā durgaṃ rāṣṭraṃ khaniṃ setuṃ vanaṃ vrajaṃ vaṇikpathaṃ cāvekṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 1.1]
śulkaṃ daṇḍaḥ pautavaṃ nāgariko lakṣaṇādhyakṣo mudrādhyakṣaḥ surā sūnā sūtraṃ tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣāraḥ sauvarṇikaḥ paṇyasaṃsthā veśyā dyūtaṃ vāstukaṃ kāruśilpigaṇo devatādhyakṣo dvārabāhirikādeyaṃ ca durgam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 2.1]
sītā bhāgo baliḥ karo vaṇik nadīpālastaro nāvaḥ pattanaṃ vivicitaṃ vartanī rajjuścorarajjuśca rāṣṭram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 3.1]
suvarṇarajatavajramaṇimuktāpravālaśaṅkhalohalavaṇabhūmiprastararasadhātavaḥ khaniḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 4.1]
puṣpaphalavāṭaṣaṇḍakedāramūlavāpāḥ setuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 5.1]
paśumṛgadravyahastivanaparigraho vanam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 6.1]

sthalapatho vāripathaśca vaṇikpathaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 8.1]
ityāyaśarīram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 9.1]
mūlyaṃ bhāgo vyājī parighaḥ kﾱptaṃ rūpikam atyayaścāyamukham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 10.1]
devapitṛpūjādānārtham svastivācanam antaḥpuram mahānasam dūtaprāvartimam koṣṭhāgāram āyudhāgāram paṇyagṛham kupyagṛham karmānto viṣṭiḥ pattyaśvarathadvipaparigraho gomaṇḍalam paśumṛgapakṣivyālavāṭāḥ kāṣṭhatṛṇavāṭāśceti vyayaśarīram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 11.1]
rājavarṣaṃ māsaḥ pakṣo divasaśca vyuṣṭam varṣāhemantagrīṣmāṇāṃ tṛtīyasaptamā divasonāḥ pakṣāḥ śeṣāḥ pūrṇāḥ pṛthagadhimāsakaḥ iti kālaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 12.1]
karaṇīyaṃ siddhaṃ śeṣam āyavyayau nīvī ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 13.1]
saṃsthānaṃ pracāraḥ śarīrāvasthāpanam ādānaṃ sarvasamudayapiṇḍaḥ saṃjātaṃ etat karaṇīyam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 14.1]
kośārpitaṃ rājahāraḥ puravyayaśca praviṣṭaṃ paramasaṃvatsarānuvṛttaṃ śāsanamuktaṃ mukhājñaptaṃ cāpātanīyaṃ etat siddham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 15.1]
siddhikarmayogaḥ daṇḍaśeṣam āharaṇīyaṃ balātkṛtapratiṣṭabdham avamṛṣṭaṃ ca praśodhyaṃ etaccheṣam asāram alpasāraṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 16.1]
vartamānaḥ paryuṣito 'nyajātaścāyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 17.1]
divasānuvṛtto vartamānaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 18.1]
paramasāṃvatsarikaḥ parapracārasaṃkrānto vā paryuṣitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 19.1]
naṣṭaprasmṛtam āyuktadaṇḍaḥ pārśvaṃ pārihīṇikam aupāyanikaṃ ḍamaragatakasvam aputrakaṃ nidhiścānyajātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 20.1]
vikṣepavyādhitāntarārambhaśeṣaṃ ca vyayapratyāyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 21.1]
vikriye paṇyānām arghavṛddhir upajā mānonmānaviśeṣo vyājī krayasaṃgharṣe vārdhavṛddhiḥ ityāyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 22.1]
nityo nityotpādiko lābho lābhotpādika iti vyayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 23.1]
divasānuvṛtto nityaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 24.1]
pakṣamāsasaṃvatsaralābho lābhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 6 25.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 7}

tatrādhikaraṇānāṃ saṃkhyāpracārasaṃjātāgram karmāntānāṃ dravyaprayogavṛddhikṣayavyayaprayāmavyājīyogasthānavetanaviṣṭipramāṇam ratnasāraphalgukupyānām arghaprativarṇakamānapratimānonmānāvamānabhāṇḍam deśagrāmajātikulasaṃghānāṃ dharmavyavahāracaritrasaṃsthānam rājopajīvināṃ pragrahapradeśabhogaparihārabhaktavetanalābham rājñaśca patnīputrāṇāṃ ratnabhūmilābhaṃ nirdeśotpātikapratīkāralābham mitrāmitrāṇāṃ ca saṃdhivigrahapradānādānaṃ nibandhapustakasthaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 2.1]

uttamamadhyamāvareṣu ca karmasu tajjātikam adhyakṣaṃ kuryāt sāmudayikeṣvavakﾱptikam vyayam upahatya rājā nānutapyeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 4.1]
sahagrāhiṇaḥ pratibhuvaḥ karmopajīvinaḥ putrā bhrātaro bhāryā duhitaro bhṛtyāścāsya karmacchedaṃ vaheyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 5.1]
triśataṃ catuḥpañcāśaccāhorātrāṇāṃ karmasaṃvatsaraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 6.1]
tam āṣāḍhīparyavasānam ūnaṃ pūrṇaṃ vā dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 7.1]
karaṇādhiṣṭhitam adhimāsakaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 8.1]
apasarpādhiṣṭhitaṃca pracāram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 9.1]
pracāracaritrasaṃsthānānyanupalabhamāno hi prakṛtaḥ samudayam ajñānena parihāpayati utthānakleśāsahatvād ālasyena śabdādiṣvindriyārtheṣu prasaktaḥ pramādena saṃkrośādharmānarthabhīrubhayena kāryārthiṣvanugrahabuddhiḥ kāmena hiṃsābuddhiḥ kopena vidyādravyavallabhāpāśrayād darpeṇa tulāmānatarkagaṇitāntaropadhānāl lobhena | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 10.1]

yathāparādham iti kauṭilyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 15.1]

yaccāgrād āyasyāntaraparṇe nīvyāṃ vardheta vyayasya vā yat parihāpayet tad aṣṭaguṇam adhyakṣaṃ dāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 19.1]
viparyaye tam eva prati syāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 20.1]

viparyaye kārmikasya dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 23.1]

akṛtāhorūpaharaṃ māsam ākāṅkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 26.1]
māsād ūrdhvaṃ māsadviśatottaraṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 27.1]

divasapañcarātrapakṣamāsacāturmāsyasaṃvatsaraiśca pratisamānayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 30.1]

vyuṣṭadeśakālamukhalābhakāraṇadeyayogapramāṇājñāpakoddhārakavidhātṛkapratigrāhakaiś ca vyayaṃ samānayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 32.1]

rājārthe kāraṇikasyāpratibadhnataḥ pratiṣedhayato vājñāṃ nibandhād āyavyayam anyathā nīvīm avalikhato dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 7 34.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 8}
kośapūrvāḥ sarvārambhāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 1.1]
tasmāt pūrvaṃ kośam avekṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 2.1]
pracārasamṛddhiścaritrānugrahaścoranigraho yuktapratiṣedhaḥ sasyasampat paṇyabāhulyam upasargapramokṣaḥ parihārakṣayo hiraṇyopāyanam iti kośavṛddhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 3.1]

tatra dvādaśaguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 19.1]
teṣāṃ haraṇopāyāścatvāriṃśat | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 20.1]
pūrvaṃ siddhaṃ paścād avatāritam paścāt siddhaṃ pūrvam avatāritam sādhyaṃ na siddham asādhyaṃ siddham siddham asiddhaṃ kṛtam asiddhaṃ siddhaṃ kṛtam alpasiddhaṃ bahu kṛtam bahusiddham alpaṃ kṛtam anyat siddham anyat kṛtam anyataḥ siddham anyataḥ kṛtam deyaṃ na dattam adeyaṃ dattam kāle na dattam akāle dattam alpaṃ dattaṃ bahu kṛtam bahu dattam alpaṃ kṛtam anyad dattam anyat kṛtam anyato dattam anyataḥ kṛtam praviṣṭam apraviṣṭaṃ kṛtam apraviṣṭaṃ praviṣṭaṃ kṛtam kupyam adattamūlyaṃ praviṣṭam dattamūlyaṃ na praviṣṭaṃ saṃkṣepo vikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ vikṣepaḥ saṃkṣepo vā mahārgham alpārgheṇa parivartitam alpārghaṃ mahārgheṇa vā samāropito 'rghaḥ pratyavaropito vā saṃvatsaro māsaviṣamaḥ kṛtaḥ māso divasaviṣamo vā samāgamaviṣamaḥ mukhaviṣamaḥ kārmikaviṣamaḥ nirvartanaviṣamaḥ piṇḍaviṣamaḥ varṇaviṣamaḥ arghaviṣamaḥ mānaviṣamaḥ māpanaviṣamaḥ bhājanaviṣamaḥ iti haraṇopāyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 21.1]
tatropayuktanidhāyakanibandhakapratigrāhakadāyakadāpakamantrivaiyāvṛtyakarān ekaikaśo 'nuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 22.1]
mithyāvāde caiṣāṃ yuktasamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 8 23.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 9}

mūlaharatādātvikakadaryāṃśca pratiṣedhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 9 20.1]

{ArthaŚ, 2, 10}

ākarādhyakṣaḥ śulbadhātuśāstrarasapākamaṇirāgajñas tajjñasakho vā tajjātakarmakaropakaraṇasampannaḥ kiṭṭamūṣāṅgārabhasmaliṅgaṃ vākaraṃ bhūtapūrvam abhūtapūrvaṃ vā bhūmiprastararasadhātum atyarthavarṇagauravam ugragandharasaṃ parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 1.1]
parvatānām abhijñātoddeśānāṃ bilaguhopatyakālayanagūḍhakhāteṣvantaḥ prasyandino jambūcūtatālaphalapakvaharidrābhedaguḍaharitālamanaḥśilākṣaudrahiṅgulukapuṇḍarīkaśukamayūrapattravarṇāḥ savarṇodakauṣadhiparyantāścikkaṇā viśadā bhārikāśca rasāḥ kāñcanikāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 2.1]
apsu niṣṭhyūtāstailavadvisarpiṇaḥ paṅkamalagrāhiṇaśca tāmrarūpyayoḥ śatād upari veddhāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 3.1]
tatpratirūpakam ugragandharasaṃ śilājatu vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 4.1]
pītakās tāmrakāstāmrapītakā vā bhūmiprastaradhātavo bhinnā nīlarājīvanto mudgamāṣakṛsaravarṇā vā dadhibindupiṇḍacitrā haridrāharītakīpadmapattraśaivalayakṛtplīhānavadyavarṇā bhinnāś cuñcuvālukālekhābindusvastikavantaḥ sugulikā arciṣmantastāpyamānā na bhidyante bahuphenadhūmāśca suvarṇadhātavaḥ pratīvāpārthās tāmrarūpyavedhanāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 5.1]
śaṅkhakarpūrasphaṭikanavanītakapotapārāvatavimalakamayūragrīvāvarṇāḥ sasyakagomedakaguḍamatsyaṇḍikāvarṇāḥ kovidārapadmapāṭalīkalāyakṣaumātasīpuṣpavarṇāḥ sasīsāḥ sāñjanā visrā bhinnāḥ śvetābhāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇābhāḥ śvetāḥ sarve vā lekhābinducitrā mṛdavo dhmāyamānā na sphuṭanti bahuphenadhūmāśca rūpyadhātavaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 6.1]
sarvadhātūnāṃ gauravavṛddhau sattvavṛddhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 7.1]
teṣām aśuddhā mūḍhagarbhā vā tīkṣṇamūtrakṣārabhāvitā rājavṛkṣavaṭapīlugopittarocanāmahiṣakharakarabhamūtraleṇḍapiṇḍabaddhās tatpratīvāpāstadavalepā vā viśuddhāḥ sravanti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 8.1]
yavamāṣatilapalāśapīlukṣārair gokṣīrājakṣīrair vā kadalīvajrakandapratīvāpo mārdavakaraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 9.1]
madhumadhukam ajāpayaḥ satailaṃ ghṛtaguḍakiṇvayutaṃ sakandalīkam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 10.1]
yad api śatasahasradhā vibhinnaṃ bhavati mṛdu tribhir eva tanniṣekaiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 10.2]
godantaśṛṅgapratīvāpo mṛdustambhanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 11.1]
bhārikaḥ snigdho mṛduśca prastaradhātur bhūmibhāgo vā piṅgalo haritaḥ pāṭalo lohito vā tāmradhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 12.1]
kākamecakaḥ kapotarocanāvarṇaḥ śvetarājinaddho vā visraḥ sīsadhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 13.1]
ūṣarakarburaḥ pakvaloṣṭavarṇo vā trapudhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 14.1]
khurumbaḥ pāṇḍurohitaḥ sinduvārapuṣpavarṇo vā tīkṣṇadhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 15.1]
kākāṇḍabhujapattravarṇo vā vaikṛntakadhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 16.1]
acchaḥ snigdhaḥ saprabho ghoṣavān śītastīvrastanurāgaśca maṇidhātuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 17.1]
dhātusamutthaṃ tajjātakarmānteṣu prayojayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 18.1]
kṛtabhāṇḍavyavahāram ekamukham atyayaṃ cānyatra kartṛkretṛvikretṝṇāṃ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 19.1]
ākarikam apaharantam aṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpayed anyatra ratnebhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 20.1]
stenam anisṛṣṭopajīvinaṃ ca baddhaṃ karma kārayet daṇḍopakāriṇaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 21.1]
vyayakriyābhārikam ākaraṃ bhāgena prakrayeṇa vā dadyāl lāghavikam ātmanā kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 22.1]
lohādhyakṣas tāmrasīsatrapuvaikṛntakārakūṭavṛttakaṃsatālalohakarmāntān kārayet lohabhāṇḍavyavahāraṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 23.1]
lakṣaṇādhyakṣaścaturbhāgatāmraṃ rūpyarūpaṃ tīkṣṇatrapusīsāñjanānām anyatamamāṣabījayuktaṃ kārayet paṇam ardhapaṇaṃ pādam aṣṭabhāgam iti pādājīvaṃ tāmrarūpaṃ māṣakam ardhamāṣakaṃ kākaṇīm ardhakākaṇīm iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 24.1]
rūpadarśakaḥ paṇayātrāṃ vyāvahārikīṃ kośapraveśyāṃ ca sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 25.1]
rūpikam aṣṭakaṃ śataṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ vyājīm pārīkṣikam aṣṭabhāgikaṃ śatam pañcaviṃśatipaṇam atyayaṃ ca anyatrakartṛkretṛvikretṛparīkṣitṛbhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 26.1]
khanyadhyakṣaḥ śaṅkhavajramaṇimuktāpravālakṣārakarmāntān kārayet paṇanavyavahāraṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 27.1]
lavaṇādhyakṣaḥ pākamuktaṃ lavaṇabhāgaṃ prakrayaṃ ca yathākālaṃ saṃgṛhṇīyād vikrayācca mūlyaṃ rūpaṃ vyājīṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 28.1]
āgantulavaṇaṃ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 29.1]
dattabhāgavibhāgasya vikrayaḥ pañcakaṃ śataṃ vyājīṃ rūpaṃ rūpikaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 30.1]
kretā śulkaṃ rājapaṇyacchedānurūpaṃ ca vaidharaṇaṃ dadyāt anyatra kretā ṣaṭchatam atyayaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 31.1]
vilavaṇam uttamaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyād anisṛṣṭopajīvī cānyatra vānaprasthebhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 32.1]
śrotriyāstapasvino viṣṭayaśca bhaktalavaṇaṃ hareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 33.1]
ato 'nyo lavaṇakṣāravargaḥ śulkaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 34.1]
evaṃ mūlyaṃ ca bhāgaṃ ca vyājīṃ parigham atyayam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 35.1]
śulkaṃ vaidharaṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ rūpaṃ rūpikam eva ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 35.2]
khanibhyo dvādaśavidhaṃ dhātuṃ paṇyaṃ ca saṃharet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 36.1]
evaṃ sarveṣu paṇyeṣu sthāpayen mukhasaṃgraham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 36.2]
ākaraprabhaḥ kośaḥ kośād daṇḍaḥ prajāyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 37.1]
pṛthivī kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ prāpyate kośabhūṣaṇā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 12 37.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 13}
suvarṇādhyakṣaḥ suvarṇarajatakarmāntānām asambandhāveśanacatuḥśālām ekadvārām akṣaśālāṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 1.1]
viśikhāmadhye sauvarṇikaṃ śilpavantam abhijātaṃ prātyayikaṃ ca sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 2.1]
jāmbūnadaṃ śātakumbhaṃ hāṭakaṃ vaiṇavaṃ śṛṅgaśuktijaṃ jātarūpaṃ rasaviddham ākarodgataṃ ca suvarṇam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 3.1]
kiñjalkavarṇaṃ mṛdu snigdham anādi bhrājiṣṇu ca śreṣṭhaṃ raktapītakaṃ madhyamaṃ raktam avaram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 4.1]
śreṣṭhānāṃ pāṇḍu śvetaṃ cāprāptakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 5.1]
tad yenāprāptakaṃ taccaturguṇena sīsena śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 6.1]
sīsānvayena bhidyamānaṃ śuṣkapaṭalair dhmāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 7.1]
rūkṣatvād bhidyamānaṃ tailagomaye niṣecayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 8.1]
ākarodgataṃ sīsānvayena bhidyamānaṃ pākapattrāṇi kṛtvā gaṇḍikāsu kuṭṭayet kadalīvajrakandakalke vā niṣecayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 9.1]
tutthodgataṃ gauḍikaṃ kāmbukaṃ cākravālikaṃ ca rūpyam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 10.1]
śvetaṃ snigdhaṃ mṛdu ca śreṣṭham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 11.1]
viparyaye sphoṭanaṃ ca duṣṭam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 12.1]
tatsīsacaturbhāgena śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 13.1]
udgatacūlikam acchaṃ bhrājiṣṇu dadhivarṇaṃ ca śuddham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 14.1]
śuddhasyaiko hāridrasya suvarṇo varṇakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 15.1]
tataḥ śulbakākaṇyuttarāpasāritā ā catuḥsīmāntād iti ṣoḍaśa varṇakāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 16.1]
suvarṇaṃ pūrvaṃ nikaṣya paścād varṇikāṃ nikaṣayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 17.1]
samarāgalekham animnonnate deśe nikaṣitaṃ parimṛditaṃ parilīḍhaṃ nakhāntarād vā gairikeṇāvacūrṇitam upadhiṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 18.1]
jātihiṅgulukena puṣpakāsīsena vā gomūtrabhāvitena digdhenāgrahastena saṃspṛṣṭaṃ suvarṇaṃ śvetībhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 19.1]
sakesaraḥ snigdho mṛdur bhrājiṣṇuśca nikaṣarāgaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 20.1]
kāliṅgakastāpīpāṣāṇo vā mudgavarṇo nikaṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 21.1]
samarāgī vikrayakrayahitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 22.1]
hasticchavikaḥ saharitaḥ pratirāgī vikrayahitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 23.1]
sthiraḥ paruṣo viṣamavarṇaścāpratirāgī krayahitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 24.1]
chedaścikkaṇaḥ samavarṇaḥ ślakṣṇo mṛdur bhrājiṣṇuśca śreṣṭhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 25.1]
tāpo bahirantaśca samaḥ kiñjalkavarṇaḥ kuraṇḍakapuṣpavarṇo vā śreṣṭhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 26.1]
śyāvo nīlaścāprāptakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 27.1]
tulāpratimānaṃ pautavādhyakṣe vakṣyāmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 28.1]
tenopadeśena rūpyasuvarṇaṃ dadyād ādadīta ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 29.1]
akṣaśālām anāyukto nopagacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 30.1]
abhigacchann ucchedyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 31.1]
āyukto vā sarūpyasuvarṇastenaiva jīyeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 32.1]
vicitavastrahastaguhyāḥ kāñcanapṛṣatatvaṣṭṛtapanīyakāravo dhmāyakacarakapāṃsudhāvakāḥ praviśeyur niṣkaseyuśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 33.1]
sarvaṃ caiṣām upakaraṇam aniṣṭhitāśca prayogāstatraivāvatiṣṭheran | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 34.1]
gṛhītaṃ suvarṇaṃ dhṛtaṃ ca prayogaṃ karaṇamadhye dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 35.1]
sāyaṃ prātaśca lakṣitaṃ kartṛkārayitṛmudrābhyāṃ nidadhyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 36.1]
kṣepaṇo guṇaḥ kṣudrakam iti karmāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 37.1]
kṣepaṇaḥ kācārpaṇādīni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 38.1]
guṇaḥ sūtravānādīni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 39.1]
ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ pṛṣatādiyuktaṃ kṣudrakam iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 40.1]
arpayet kācakarmaṇaḥ pañcabhāgaṃ kāñcanaṃ daśabhāgaṃ kaṭumānam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 41.1]
tāmrapādayuktaṃ rūpyaṃ rūpyapādayuktaṃ vā suvarṇaṃ saṃskṛtakaṃ tasmād rakṣet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 42.1]
pṛṣatakācakarmaṇaḥ trayo hi bhāgāḥ paribhāṇḍaṃ dvau vāstukaṃ catvāro vā vāstukaṃ trayaḥ paribhāṇḍam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 43.1]
tvaṣṭṛkarmaṇaḥ śulbabhāṇḍaṃ samasuvarṇena saṃyūhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 44.1]
rūpyabhāṇḍaṃ ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ vā suvarṇārdhenāvalepayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 45.1]
caturbhāgasuvarṇaṃ vā vālukāhiṅgulukasya rasena cūrṇena vā vāsayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 46]
tapanīyaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ suvarṇaṃ surāgaṃ samasīsātikrāntaṃ pākapattrapakvaṃ saindhavikayojjvālitaṃ nīlapītaśvetaharitaśukapattravarṇānāṃ prakṛtir bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 47]
tīkṣṇaṃ cāsya mayūragrīvābhaṃ śvetabhaṅgaṃ cimicimāyitaṃ pītacūrṇitaṃ kākaṇikaḥ suvarṇarāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 48.1]
tāram upaśuddhaṃ vā asthitutthe catuḥ samasīse catuḥ śuṣkatutthe catuḥ kapāle trir gomaye dvir evaṃ saptadaśatutthātikrāntaṃ saindhavikayojjvālitam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 49.1]
etasmāt kākaṇyuttaramād vimāṣād iti suvarṇe deyaṃ paścād rāgayogaḥ śvetatāraṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 50]
trayo 'ṃśāstapanīyasya dvātriṃśadbhāgaśvetatāramūrchitās tat śvetalohitakaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 51]
tāmraṃ pītakaṃ karoti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 52.1]
tapanīyam ujjvālya rāgatribhāgaṃ dadyāt pītarāgaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 53.1]
śvetatārabhāgau dvāvekastapanīyasya mudgavarṇaṃ karoti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 54.1]
kālāyasasyārdhabhāgābhyaktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 55.1]
pratilepinā rasena dviguṇābhyaktaṃ tapanīyaṃ śukapattravarṇaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 56.1]
tasyārambhe rāgaviśeṣeṣu prativarṇikāṃ gṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 57.1]
tīkṣṇatāmrasaṃskāraṃ ca budhyeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 58.1]
tasmād vajramaṇimuktāpravālarūpāṇām apaneyimānaṃ ca rūpyasuvarṇabhāṇḍabandhapramāṇāni ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 59.1]
samarāgaṃ samadvandvam asaktapṛṣataṃ sthiram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 60.1]
supramṛṣṭam asampītaṃ vibhaktaṃ dhāraṇe sukham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 60.2]
abhinītaṃ prabhāyuktaṃ saṃsthānamadhuraṃ samam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 61.1]
manonetrābhirāmaṃ ca tapanīyaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 13 61.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 14}
sauvarṇikaḥ paurajānapadānāṃ rūpyasuvarṇam āveśanibhiḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 1.1]
nirdiṣṭakālakāryaṃ ca karma kuryur anirdiṣṭakālaṃ kāryāpadeśam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 2.1]
kāryasyānyathākaraṇe vetananāśas taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 3.1]
kālātipātane pādahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 4.1]
yathāvarṇapramāṇaṃ nikṣepaṃ gṛhṇīyus tathāvidham evārpayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 5.1]
kālāntarād api ca tathāvidham eva pratigṛhṇīyuḥ anyatra kṣīṇapariśīrṇābhyām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 6.1]
āveśanibhiḥ suvarṇapudgalalakṣaṇaprayogeṣu tattajjānīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 7.1]
taptakaladhautakayoḥ kākaṇikaḥ suvarṇe kṣayo deyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 8.1]
tīkṣṇakākaṇī rūpyadviguṇaḥ rāgaprakṣepas tasya ṣaḍbhāgaḥ kṣayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 9.1]
varṇahīne māṣāvare pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ pramāṇahīne madhyamas tulāpratimānopadhāv uttamaḥ kṛtabhāṇḍopadhau ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 10.1]
sauvarṇikenādṛṣṭam anyatra vā prayogaṃ kārayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 11.1]
kartur dviguṇaḥ sāpasāraścet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 12.1]
anapasāraḥ kaṇṭakaśodhanāya nīyeta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 13.1]
kartuśca dviśato daṇḍaḥ paṇacchedanaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 14.1]
tulāpratimānabhāṇḍaṃ pautavahastāt krīṇīyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 15.1]
anyathā dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 16.1]
ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ saṃyūhyam avalepyaṃ saṃghātyaṃ vāsitakaṃ ca kārukarma | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 17.1]
tulāviṣamam apasāraṇaṃ visrāvaṇaṃ peṭakaḥ piṅkaśceti haraṇopāyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 18.1]
saṃnāminyutkīrṇikā bhinnamastakopakaṇṭhī kuśikyā sakaṭukakṣyā parivelyāyaskāntā ca duṣṭatulāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 19.1]
rūpyasya dvau bhāgāvekaḥ śulbasya tripuṭakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 20.1]
tenākarod gatam apasāryate tattripuṭakāpasāritam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 21.1]
śulbena śulbāpasāritaṃ vellakena vellakāpasāritaṃ śulbārdhasāreṇa hemnā hemāpasāritam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 22.1]
mūkamūṣā pūtikiṭṭaḥ karaṭukamukhaṃ nālī saṃdaṃśo joṅganī suvarcikālavaṇaṃ tad eva suvarṇam ityapasāraṇamārgāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 23.1]
pūrvapraṇihitā vā piṇḍavālukā mūṣābhedād agniṣṭhād uddhriyante | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 24.1]
paścād bandhane ācitakapattraparīkṣāyāṃ vā rūpyarūpeṇa parivartanaṃ visrāvaṇam piṇḍavālukānāṃ lohapiṇḍavālukābhir vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 25.1]
gāḍhaścābhyuddhāryaśca peṭakaḥ saṃyūhyāvalepyasaṃghātyeṣu kriyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 26.1]
sīsarūpaṃ suvarṇapattreṇāvaliptam abhyantaram aṣṭakena baddhaṃ gāḍhapeṭakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 27.1]
sa eva paṭalasampuṭeṣvabhyuddhāryaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 28.1]
pattram āśliṣṭaṃ yamakapattraṃ vāvalepyeṣu kriyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 29.1]
śulbaṃ tāraṃ vā garbhaḥ pattrāṇāṃ saṃghātyeṣu kriyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 30.1]
śulbarūpaṃ suvarṇapattrasaṃhataṃ pramṛṣṭaṃ supārśvaṃ tad eva yamakapattrasaṃhataṃ pramṛṣṭaṃ tāmratārarūpaṃ cottaravarṇakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 31.1]
tad ubhayaṃ tāpanikaṣābhyāṃ niḥśabdollekhanābhyāṃ vā vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 32.1]
abhyuddhāryaṃ badarāmle lavaṇodake vā sādayanti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 33.1]
ghane suṣire vā rūpe suvarṇamṛnmālukāhiṅgulukakalpo vā tapto 'vatiṣṭhate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 34.1]
dṛḍhavāstuke vā rūpe vālukāmiśraṃ jatu gāndhārapaṅko vā tapto 'vatiṣṭhate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 35.1]
tayostāpanam avadhvaṃsanaṃ vā śuddhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 36.1]
saparibhāṇḍe vā rūpe lavaṇam ulkayā kaṭuśarkarayā taptam avatiṣṭhate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 37.1]
tasya kvāthanaṃ śuddhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 38.1]
abhrapaṭalam aṣṭakena dviguṇavāstuke vā rūpe badhyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 39.1]
tasyāpihitakācakasyodake nimajjata ekadeśaḥ sīdati paṭalāntareṣu vā sūcyā bhidyate | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 40.1]
maṇayo rūpyaṃ suvarṇaṃ vā ghanasuṣirāṇāṃ piṅkaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 41.1]
tasya tāpanam avadhvaṃsanaṃ vā śuddhir iti piṅkaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 42.1]
tasmād vajramaṇimuktāpravālarūpāṇāṃ jātirūpavarṇapramāṇapudgalalakṣaṇānyupalabheta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 43.1]
kṛtabhāṇḍaparīkṣāyāṃ purāṇabhāṇḍapratisaṃskāre vā catvāro haraṇopāyāḥ parikuṭṭanam avacchedanam ullekhanaṃ parimardanaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 44.1]
peṭakāpadeśena pṛṣataṃ guṇaṃ piṭakāṃ vā yat pariśātayanti tatparikuṭṭanam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 45.1]
yaddviguṇavāstukānāṃ vā rūpe sīsarūpaṃ prakṣipyābhyantaram avacchindanti tad avacchedanam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 46.1]
yad ghanānāṃ tīkṣṇenollikhanti tad ullekhanam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 47.1]
haritālamanaḥśilāhiṅgulukacūrṇānām anyatamena kuruvindacūrṇena vā vastraṃ saṃyūhya yat parimṛdnanti tat parimardanam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 48.1]
tena sauvarṇarājatāni bhāṇḍāni kṣīyante na caiṣāṃ kiṃcid avarugṇaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 49.1]
bhagnakhaṇḍaghṛṣṭānāṃ saṃyūhyānāṃ sadṛśenānumānaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 50.1]
virūpāṇāṃ vā tāpanam udakapeṣaṇaṃ ca bahuśaḥ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 51.1]
avakṣepaḥ pratimānam agnir gaṇḍikā bhaṇḍikādhikaraṇī piñchaḥ sūtraṃ cellaṃ bollanaṃ śira utsaṅgo makṣikā svakāyekṣā dṛtir udakaśarāvam agniṣṭham iti kācaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 52.1]
rājatānāṃ visraṃ malagrāhi paruṣaṃ prastīnaṃ vivarṇaṃ vā duṣṭam iti vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 53.1]
evaṃ navaṃ ca jīrṇaṃ ca virūpaṃ cāpi bhāṇḍakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 54.1]
parīkṣetātyayaṃ caiṣāṃ yathoddiṣṭaṃ prakalpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 14 54.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 15}
koṣṭhāgārādhyakṣaḥ sītārāṣṭrakrayimaparivartakaprāmityakāpamityakasaṃhanikānyajātavyayapratyāyopasthānāny upalabhet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 1.1]
sītādhyakṣopanītaḥ sasyavarṇakaḥ sītā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 2.1]
piṇḍakaraḥ ṣaḍbhāgaḥ senābhaktaṃ baliḥ kara utsaṅgaḥ pārśvaṃ pārihīṇikam aupāyanikaṃ kauṣṭheyakaṃ ca rāṣṭram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 3.1]
dhānyamūlyaṃ kośanirhāraḥ prayogapratyādānaṃ ca krayimam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 4.1]
sasyavarṇānām arghāntareṇa vinimayaḥ parivartakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 5.1]
sasyayācanam anyataḥ prāmityakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 6.1]
tad eva pratidānārtham āpamityakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 7.1]
kuṭṭakarocakasaktuśuktapiṣṭakarma tajjīvaneṣu tailapīḍanam audracākrikeṣvikṣūṇāṃ ca kṣārakarma saṃhanikā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 8.1]
naṣṭaprasmṛtādir anyajātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 9.1]
vikṣepavyādhitāntarārambhaśeṣaṃ ca vyayapratyāyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 10.1]
tulāmānāntaraṃ hastapūraṇam utkaro vyājī paryuṣitaṃ prārjitaṃ copasthānam iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 11.1]
dhānyasnehakṣāralavaṇānāṃ dhānyakalpaṃ sītādhyakṣe vakṣyāmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 12.1]
sarpistailavasāmajjānaḥ snehāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 13.1]
phāṇitaguḍamatsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarāḥ kṣāravargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 14.1]
saindhavasāmudrabiḍayavakṣārasauvarcalodbhedajā lavaṇavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 15.1]
kṣaudraṃ mārdvīkaṃ ca madhu | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 16.1]
ikṣurasaguḍamadhuphāṇitajāmbavapanasānām anyatamo meṣaśṛṅgīpippalīkvāthābhiṣuto māsikaḥ ṣāṇmāsikaḥ sāṃvatsariko vā cidbhiṭorvārukekṣukāṇḍāmraphalāmalakāvasutaḥ śuddho vā śuktavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 17.1]
vṛkṣāmlakaramardāmravidalāmalakamātuluṅgakolabadarasauvīrakaparūṣakādiḥ phalāmlavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 18.1]
dadhidhānyāmlādir dravāmlavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 19.1]
pippalīmaricaśṛṅgiberājājīkirātatiktagaurasarṣapakustumburucorakadamanakamaruvakaśigrukāṇḍādiḥ kaṭukavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 20.1]
śuṣkamatsyamāṃsakandamūlaphalaśākādi ca śākavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 21.1]
tato 'rdham āpadarthaṃ jānapadānāṃ sthāpayed ardham upayuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 22.1]
navena cānavaṃ śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 23.1]
kṣuṇṇaghṛṣṭapiṣṭabhṛṣṭānām ārdraśuṣkasiddhānāṃ ca dhānyānāṃ vṛddhikṣayapramāṇāni pratyakṣīkurvīta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 24.1]
kodravavrīhīṇām ardhaṃ sāraḥ śālīnām ardhabhāgonaḥ tribhāgono varakāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 25.1]
priyaṅgūṇām ardhaṃ sāro navabhāgavṛddhiśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 26.1]
udārakastulyaḥ yavā godhūmāśca kṣuṇṇāḥ tilā yavā mudgamāṣāśca ghṛṣṭāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 27.1]
pañcabhāgavṛddhirgodhūmaḥ saktavaśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 28.1]
pādonā kalāyacamasī | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 29.1]
mudgamāṣāṇām ardhapādonā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 30.1]
śaumbyānām ardhaṃ sāraḥ tribhāgono masūrāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 31.1]
piṣṭam āmaṃ kulmāṣāścādhyardhaguṇāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 32.1]
dviguṇo yāvakaḥ pulākaḥ piṣṭaṃ ca siddham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 33.1]
kodravavarakodārakapriyaṅgūṇāṃ triguṇam annam caturguṇaṃ vrīhīṇām pañcaguṇaṃ śālīnām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 34.1]
timitam aparānnaṃ dviguṇam ardhādhikaṃ virūḍhānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 35.1]
pañcabhāgavṛddhir bhṛṣṭānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 36.1]
kalāyo dviguṇaḥ lājā bharujāśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 37.1]
ṣaṭkaṃ tailam atasīnām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 38.1]
nimbakuśāmrakapitthādīnāṃ pañcabhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 39.1]
caturbhāgikās tilakusumbhamadhūkeṅgudīsnehāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 40.1]
kārpāsakṣaumāṇāṃ pañcapale palaṃ sūtram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 41.1]
pañcadroṇe śālīnāṃ dvādaśāḍhakaṃ taṇḍulānāṃ kalabhabhojanam ekādaśakaṃ vyālānām daśakam aupavāhyānāṃ navakaṃ sāṃnāhyānām aṣṭakaṃ pattīnām saptakaṃ mukhyānām ṣaṭkaṃ devīkumārāṇām pañcakaṃ rājñām akhaṇḍapariśuddhānāṃ vā taṇḍulānāṃ prasthaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 42.1]
taṇḍulānāṃ prasthaḥ caturbhāgaḥ sūpaḥ sūpaṣoḍaśo lavaṇasyāṃśaḥ caturbhāgaḥ sarpiṣastailasya vaikam āryabhaktaṃ puṃsaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 43.1]
ṣaḍbhāgaḥ sūpaḥ ardhasneham avarāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 44.1]
pādonaṃ strīṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 45.1]
ardhaṃ bālānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 46.1]
māṃsapalaviṃśatyā snehārdhakuḍubaḥ paliko lavaṇasyāṃśaḥ kṣārapalayogo dvidharaṇikaḥ kaṭukayogo dadhnaś cārdhaprasthaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 47.1]
tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 48.1]
śākānām adhyardhaguṇaḥ śuṣkāṇāṃ dviguṇaḥ sa caiva yogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 49.1]
hastyaśvayos tadadhyakṣe vidhāpramāṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 50.1]
balīvardānāṃ māṣadroṇaṃ yavānāṃ vā pulākaḥ śeṣam aśvavidhānam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 51.1]
viśeṣo ghāṇapiṇyākatulā kaṇakuṇḍakaṃ daśāḍhakaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 52.1]
dviguṇaṃ mahiṣoṣṭrāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 53.1]
ardhadroṇaṃ kharapṛṣatarohitānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 54.1]
āḍhakam eṇakuraṅgāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 55.1]
ardhāḍhakam ajaiḍakavarāhāṇām dviguṇaṃ vā kaṇakuṇḍakam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 56.1]
prasthaudanaḥ śunām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 57.1]
haṃsakrauñcamayūrāṇām ardhaprasthaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 58.1]
śeṣāṇām ato mṛgapaśupakṣivyālānām ekabhaktād anumānaṃ grāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 59.1]
aṅgārāṃstuṣān lohakarmāntabhittilepyānāṃ hārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 60.1]
kaṇikā dāsakarmakarasūpakārāṇām ato 'nyad audanikāpūpikebhyaḥ prayacchet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 61.1]
tulāmānabhāṇḍaṃ rocanīdṛṣanmusalolūkhalakuṭṭakarocakayantrapattrakaśūrpacālanikākaṇḍolīpiṭakasaṃmārjanyaś copakaraṇāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 62.1]
mārjakarakṣakadharakamāyakamāpakadāyakadāpakaśalākāpratigrāhakadāsakarmakaravargaśca viṣṭiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 63.1]
uccair dhānyasya nikṣepo mūtāḥ kṣārasya saṃhatāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 64.1]
mṛtkāṣṭhakoṣṭhāḥ snehasya pṛthivī lavaṇasya ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 15 64.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 16}
paṇyādhyakṣaḥ sthalajalajānāṃ nānāvidhānāṃ paṇyānāṃ sthalapathavāripathopayātānāṃ sāraphalgvarghāntaraṃ priyāpriyatāṃ ca vidyāt tathā vikṣepasaṃkṣepakrayavikrayaprayogakālān | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 1.1]
yacca paṇyaṃ pracuraṃ syāt tad ekīkṛtyārgham āropayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 2.1]
prāpte 'rghe vārghāntaraṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 3.1]
svabhūmijānāṃ rājapaṇyānām ekamukhaṃ vyavahāraṃ sthāpayet parabhūmijānām anekamukham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 4.1]
ubhayaṃ ca prajānām anugraheṇa vikrāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 5.1]
sthūlam api ca lābhaṃ prajānām aupaghātikaṃ vārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 6.1]
ajasrapaṇyānāṃ kāloparodhaṃ saṃkuladoṣaṃ vā notpādayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 7.1]
bahumukhaṃ vā rājapaṇyaṃ vaidehakāḥ kṛtārghaṃ vikrīṇīran | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 8.1]
chedānurūpaṃ ca vaidharaṇaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 9.1]
ṣoḍaśabhāgo mānavyājī viṃśatibhāgastulāmānam gaṇyapaṇyānām ekādaśabhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 10.1]
parabhūmijaṃ paṇyam anugraheṇāvāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 11.1]
nāvikasārthavāhebhyaśca parihāram āyatikṣamaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 12.1]
anabhiyogaś cārtheṣvāgantūnām anyatra sabhyopakāribhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 13.1]
paṇyādhiṣṭhātāraḥ paṇyamūlyam ekamukhaṃ kāṣṭhadroṇyām ekacchidrāpidhānāyāṃ nidadhyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 14.1]
ahnaścāṣṭame bhāge paṇyādhyakṣasyārpayeyuḥ idaṃ vikrītam idaṃ śeṣam iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 15.1]
tulāmānabhāṇḍaṃ cārpayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 16.1]
iti svaviṣaye vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 17.1]
paraviṣaye tu paṇyapratipaṇyayor arghaṃ mūlyaṃ cāgamayya śulkavartanyātivāhikagulmataradeyabhaktabhāgavyayaśuddham udayaṃ paśyet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 18.1]
asaty udaye bhāṇḍanirvahaṇena paṇyapratipaṇyānayanena vā lābhaṃ paśyet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 19.1]
tataḥ sārapādena sthalavyavahāram adhvanā kṣemeṇa prayojayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 20.1]
aṭavyantapālapurarāṣṭramukhyaiśca pratisaṃsargaṃ gacched anugrahārtham | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 21.1]
āpadi sāram ātmānaṃ vā mokṣayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 22.1]
ātmano vā bhūmiṃ prāptaḥ sarvadeyaviśuddhaṃ vyavahareta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 23.1]
vāripathe vā yānabhāgakapathyadanapaṇyapratipaṇyārghapramāṇayātrākālabhayapratīkārapaṇyapattanacāritrāṇy upalabheta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 24.1]
nadīpathe ca vijñāya vyavahāraṃ caritrataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 25.1]
yato lābhastato gacched alābhaṃ parivarjayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 16 25.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 17}
kupyādhyakṣo dravyavanapālaiḥ kupyam ānāyayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 1.1]
dravyavanakarmāntāṃśca prayojayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 2.1]
dravyavanacchidāṃ ca deyam atyayaṃ ca sthāpayed anyatrāpadbhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 3.1]
kupyavargaḥ śākatiniśadhanvanārjunamadhūkatilakasālaśiṃśapārimedarājādanaśirīṣakhadirasaralatālasarjāśvakarṇasomavalkakuśāmrapriyakadhavādiḥ sāradāruvargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 4.1]
uṭajacimiyacāpaveṇuvaṃśasātinakaṇṭakabhāllūkādir veṇuvargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 5.1]
vetraśīkavallīvāśīśyāmalatānāgalatādir vallīvargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 6.1]
mālatīmūrvārkaśaṇagavedhukātasyādir valkavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 7.1]
muñjabalbajādi rajjubhāṇḍam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 8.1]
tālītālabhūrjānāṃ pattram | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 9.1]
kiṃśukakusumbhakuṅkumānāṃ puṣpam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 10.1]
kandamūlaphalādir auṣadhavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 11.1]
kālakūṭavatsanābhahālāhalameṣaśṛṅgamustākuṣṭhamahāviṣavellitakagaurārdrabālakamārkaṭahaimavatakāliṅgakadāradakāṅkolasārakoṣṭrakādīni viṣāṇi sarpāḥ kīṭāśca ta eva kumbhagatāḥ viṣavargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 12.1]
godhāserakadvīpyṛkṣaśiṃśumārasiṃhavyāghrahastimahiṣacamarasṛmarakhaḍgagomṛgagavayānāṃ carmāsthipittasnāyvakṣidantaśṛṅgakhurapucchāni anyeṣāṃ vāpi mṛgapaśupakṣivyālānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 13.1]
kālāyasatāmravṛttakaṃsasīsatrapuvaikṛntakārakūṭāni lohāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 14.1]
vidalamṛttikāmayaṃ bhāṇḍam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 15.1]
aṅgāratuṣabhasmāni mṛgapaśupakṣivyālavāṭāḥ kāṣṭhatṛṇavāṭāś ceti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 16.1]
bahir antaśca karmāntā vibhaktāḥ sārvabhāṇḍikāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 17.1]
ājīvapurarakṣārthāḥ kāryāḥ kupyopajīvinā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 17 17.2]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 18}
āyudhāgārādhyakṣaḥ sāṃgrāmikaṃ daurgakarmikaṃ parapurābhighātikaṃ ca yantram āyudham āvaraṇam upakaraṇaṃ ca tajjātakāruśilpibhiḥ kṛtakarmapramāṇakālavetanaphalaniṣpattibhiḥ kārayet svabhūmiṣu ca sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 1.1]
sthānaparivartanam ātapapravātapradānaṃ ca bahuśaḥ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 2.1]
ūṣmopasnehakrimibhir upahanyamānam anyathā sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 3.1]
jātirūpalakṣaṇapramāṇāgamamūlyanikṣepaiścopalabheta | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 4.1]
sarvatobhadrajāmadagnyabahumukhaviśvāsaghātisaṃghāṭīyānakaparjanyakabāhūrdhvabāhvardhabāhūni sthitayantrāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 5.1]
pāñcālikadevadaṇḍasūkarikāmusalayaṣṭihastivārakatālavṛntamudgaragadāspṛktalākuddālāsphāṭimotpāṭimodghāṭimaśataghnitriśūlacakrāṇi calayantrāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 6.1]
śaktiprāsakuntahāṭakabhiṇḍipālaśūlatomaravarāhakarṇakaṇayakarpaṇatrāsikādīni ca hulamukhāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 7.1]
tālacāpadāravaśārṅgāṇi kārmukakodaṇḍadrūṇā dhanūṃṣi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 8.1]
mūrvārkaśaṇagavedhuveṇusnāyūni jyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 9.1]
veṇuśaraśalākādaṇḍāsananārācāś ceṣavaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 10.1]
teṣāṃ mukhāni chedanabhedanatāḍanāny āyasāsthidāravāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 11.1]
nistriṃśamaṇḍalāgrāsiyaṣṭayaḥ khaḍgāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 12.1]
khaḍgamahiṣavāraṇaviṣāṇadāruveṇumūlāni tsaravaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 13.1]
paraśukuṭhārapaṭṭasakhanitrakuddālakrakacakāṇḍacchedanāḥ kṣurakalpāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 14.1]
yantragoṣpaṇamuṣṭipāṣāṇarocanīdṛṣadaś cāśmāyudhāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 15.1]
lohajālikāpaṭṭakavacasūtrakaṅkaṭaśiṃśumārakakhaḍgidhenukahastigocarmakhuraśṛṅgasaṃghātaṃ varmāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 16.1]
śirastrāṇakaṇṭhatrāṇakūrpāsakañcukavāravāṇapaṭṭanāgodarikāḥ peṭīcarmahastikarṇatālamūladhamanikākapāṭakiṭikāpratihatabalāhakāntāś cāvaraṇāṇi | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 17.1]
hastirathavājināṃ yogyabhāṇḍam ālaṃkārikaṃ saṃnāhakalpanāś copakaraṇāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 18.1]
aindrajālikam aupaniṣadikaṃ ca karma | [ArthaŚ, 2, 18 19.1]
