{ArthaŚ, 2, 19}
pautavādhyakṣaḥ pautavakarmāntān kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 1.1]
dhānyamāṣā daśa suvarṇamāṣakaḥ pañca vā guñjāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 2.1]
te ṣoḍaśa suvarṇaḥ karṣo vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 3.1]
catuṣkarṣaṃ palam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 4.1]
aṣṭāśītir gaurasarṣapā rūpyamāṣakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 5.1]
te ṣoḍaśa dharaṇaṃ śaimbyāni vā viṃśatiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 6.1]
viṃśatitaṇḍulaṃ vajradharaṇam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 7.1]
ardhamāṣakaḥ māṣakaḥ dvau catvāraḥ aṣṭau māṣakāḥ suvarṇo dvau catvāraḥ aṣṭau suvarṇāḥ daśa viṃśatiḥ triṃśat catvāriṃśat śatam iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 8.1]
tena dharaṇāni vyākhyātāni | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 9.1]
pratimānānyayomayāni māgadhamekalaśailamayāni yāni vā nodakapradehābhyāṃ vṛddhiṃ gaccheyur uṣṇena vā hrāsam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 10.1]
ṣaḍaṅgulād ūrdhvam aṣṭāṅgulottarā daśa tulāḥ kārayel lohapalād ūrdhvam ekapalottarāḥ yantram ubhayataḥśikyaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 11.1]
pañcatriṃśatpalalohāṃ dvisaptatyaṅgulāyāmāṃ samavṛttāṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 12.1]
tasyāḥ pañcapalikaṃ maṇḍalaṃ baddhvā samakaraṇaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 13.1]
tataḥ karṣottaraṃ palaṃ palottaraṃ daśapalaṃ dvādaśa pañcadaśa viṃśatir iti padāni kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 14.1]
tata āśatād daśottaraṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 15.1]
akṣeṣu nāndīpinaddhaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 16.1]
dviguṇalohāṃ tulām ataḥ ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulāyāmāṃ parimāṇīṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 17.1]
tasyāḥ śatapadād ūrdhvaṃ viṃśatiḥ pañcāśat śatam iti padāni kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 18.1]
viṃśatitauliko bhāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 19.1]
daśadhāraṇikaṃ palam | [ArthaŚ, 2, 19 20.1]
{ArthaŚ, 2, 25}
surādhyakṣaḥ surākiṇvavyavahārān durge janapade skandhāvāre vā tajjātasurākiṇvavyavahāribhiḥ kārayed ekamukham anekamukhaṃ vā vikrayakrayavaśena vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 1.1]
ṣaṭśatam atyayam anyatra kartṛkretṛvikretṝṇāṃ sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 2.1]
grāmād anirṇayaṇam asaṃpātaṃ ca surāyāḥ pramādabhayāt karmasu nirdiṣṭānām maryādātikramabhayād āryāṇām utsāhabhayācca tīkṣṇānām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 3.1]
lakṣitam alpaṃ vā caturbhāgam ardhakuḍubaṃ kuḍubam ardhaprasthaṃ prasthaṃ veti jñātaśaucā nirhareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 4.1]
pānāgāreṣu vā pibeyur asaṃcāriṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 5.1]
nikṣepopanidhiprayogāpahṛtānām aniṣṭopagatānāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ jñānārtham asvāmikaṃ kupyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ copalabhya nikṣeptāram anyatra vyapadeśena grāhayed ativyayakartāram anāyativyayaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 6.1]
na cānargheṇa kālikāṃ vā surāṃ dadyād anyatra duṣṭasurāyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 7.1]
tām anyatra vikrāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 8.1]
dāsakarmakarebhyo vā vetanaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 9.1]
vāhanapratipānaṃ sūkarapoṣaṇaṃ vā dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 10.1]
pānāgārāṇyanekakakṣyāṇi vibhaktaśayanāsanavanti pānoddeśāni gandhamālyodakavanti ṛtusukhāni kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 11.1]
tatrasthāḥ prakṛtyautpattikau vyayau gūḍhā vidyuḥ āgantūṃśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 12.1]
kretṝṇāṃ mattasuptānām alaṅkārācchādanahiraṇyāni ca vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 13.1]
tannāśe vaṇijastacca tāvacca daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 14.1]
vaṇijastu saṃvṛteṣu kakṣyāvibhāgeṣu svadāsībhiḥ peśalarūpābhir āgantūnāṃ vāstavyānāṃ cāryarūpāṇāṃ mattasuptānāṃ bhāvaṃ vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 15.1]
medakaprasannāsavāriṣṭamaireyamadhūnām | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 16.1]
udakadroṇaṃ taṇḍulānām ardhāḍhakaṃ trayaḥ prasthāḥ kiṇvasyeti medakayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 17.1]
dvādaśāḍhakaṃ piṣṭasya pañca prasthāḥ kiṇvasya kramukatvakphalayukto vā jātisambhāraḥ prasannāyogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 18.1]
kapitthatulā phāṇitaṃ pañcataulikaṃ prastho madhuna ityāsavayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 19.1]
pādādhiko jyeṣṭhaḥ pādahīnaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 20.1]
cikitsakapramāṇāḥ pratyekaśo vikārāṇām ariṣṭāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 21.1]
meṣaśṛṅgītvakkvāthābhiṣuto guḍapratīvāpaḥ pippalīmaricasambhārastriphalāyukto vā maireyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 22.1]
guḍayuktānāṃ vā sarveṣāṃ triphalāsambhāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 23.1]
mṛdvīkāraso madhu | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 24.1]
tasya svadeśo vyākhyānaṃ kāpiśāyanaṃ hārahūrakam iti | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 25.1]
māṣakalanīdroṇamāmaṃ siddhaṃ vā tribhāgādhikataṇḍulaṃ moraṭādīnāṃ kārṣikabhāgayuktaṃ kiṇvabandhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 26.1]
pāṭhālodhratejovatyelāvālukamadhukamadhurasāpriyaṅgudāruharidrāmaricapippalīnāṃ ca pañcakārṣikaḥ sambhārayogo medakasya prasannāyāśca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 27.1]
madhukaniryūhayuktā kaṭaśarkarā varṇaprasādanī ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 28.1]
cocacitrakavilaṅgagajapippalīnāṃ ca kārṣikaḥ kramukamadhukamustālodhrāṇāṃ dvikārṣikaścāsavasambhāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 29.1]
daśabhāgaścaiṣāṃ bījabandhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 30.1]
prasannāyogaḥ śvetasurāyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 31.1]
sahakārasurā rasottarā bījottarā vā mahāsurā saṃbhārikī vā | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 32.1]
tāsāṃ moraṭāpalāśapattūrameṣaśṛṅgīkarañjakṣīravṛkṣakaṣāyabhāvitaṃ dagdhakaṭaśarkarācūrṇaṃ lodhracitrakavilaṅgapāṭhāmustākaliṅgayavadāruharidrendīvaraśatapuṣpāpāmārgasaptaparṇanimbāsphotakalkārdhayuktam antarnakho muṣṭiḥ kumbhīṃ rājapeyāṃ prasādayati | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 33.1]
phāṇitaḥ pañcapalikaścātra rasavṛddhir deyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 34.1]
kuṭumbinaḥ kṛtyeṣu śvetasurām auṣadhārthaṃ vāriṣṭam anyad vā kartuṃ labheran | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 35.1]
utsavasamājayātrāsu caturahaḥ sauriko deyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 36.1]
teṣvananujñātānāṃ prahavanāntaṃ daivasikam atyayaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 37.1]
surākiṇvavicayaṃ striyo bālāśca kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 38.1]
arājapaṇyāḥ pañcakaṃ śataṃ śulkaṃ dadyuḥ surakāmedakāriṣṭamadhuphalāmlāmlaśīdhūnāṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 39.1]
ahnaśca vikrayaṃ jñātvā vyājīṃ mānahiraṇyayoḥ | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 40.1]
tathā vaidharaṇaṃ kuryād ucitaṃ cānuvartayet | [ArthaŚ, 2, 25 40.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 1}
pradeṣṭārastrayastrayo 'mātyāḥ kaṇṭakaśodhanaṃ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 1.1]
arthyapratīkārāḥ kāruśāsitāraḥ saṃnikṣeptāraḥ svavittakāravaḥ śreṇīpramāṇā nikṣepaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 2.1]
vipattau śreṇī nikṣepaṃ bhajeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 3.1]
nirdiṣṭadeśakālakāryaṃ ca karma kuryuḥ anirdiṣṭadeśakālaṃ kāryāpadeśam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 4.1]
kālātipātane pādahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 5.1]
anyatra bhreṣopanipātābhyāṃ naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ vābhyāvaheyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 6.1]
kāryasyānyathākaraṇe vetananāśastaddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 7.1]
tantuvāyā daśaikādaśikaṃ sūtraṃ vardhayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 8.1]
vṛddhicchede chedadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 9.1]
sūtramūlyaṃ vānavetanaṃ kṣaumakauśeyānām adhyardhaguṇaṃ pattrorṇākambaladukūlānāṃ dviguṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 10.1]
mānahīne hīnāvahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍas tulāhīne hīnacaturguṇo daṇḍaḥ sūtraparivartane mūlyadviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 11.1]
tena dvipaṭavānaṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 12.1]
ūrṇātulāyāḥ pañcapaliko vihananacchedo romacchedaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 13.1]
rajakāḥ kāṣṭhaphalakaślakṣṇaśilāsu vastrāṇi nenijyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 14.1]
anyatra nenijato vastropaghātaṃ ṣaṭpaṇaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 15.1]
mudgarāṅkād anyad vāsaḥ paridadhānāstripaṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 16.1]
paravastravikrayāvakrayādhāneṣu ca dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ parivartane mūlyadviguṇo vastradānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 17.1]
mukulāvadātaṃ śilāpaṭṭaśuddhaṃ dhautasūtravarṇaṃ pramṛṣṭaśvetaṃ caikarātrottaraṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 18.1]
pañcarātrikaṃ tanurāgaṃ ṣaḍrātrikaṃ nīlaṃ puṣpalākṣāmañjiṣṭhāraktaṃ guruparikarma yatnopacāryaṃ jātyaṃ vāsaḥ saptarātrikam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 19.1]
tataḥ paraṃ vetanahāniṃ prāpnuyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 20.1]
śraddheyā rāgavivādeṣu vetanaṃ kuśalāḥ kalpayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 21.1]
parārdhyānāṃ paṇo vetanaṃ madhyamānām ardhapaṇaḥ pratyavarāṇāṃ pādaḥ sthūlakānāṃ māṣakadvimāṣakaṃ dviguṇaṃ raktakānām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 22.1]
prathamanejane caturbhāgaḥ kṣayaḥ dvitīye pañcabhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 23.1]
tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 24.1]
rajakaistunnavāyā vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 25.1]
suvarṇakārāṇām aśucihastād rūpyaṃ suvarṇam anākhyāya sarūpaṃ krīṇatāṃ dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍo virūpaṃ caturviṃśatipaṇaś corahastād aṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 26.1]
pracchannavirūpamūlyahīnakrayeṣu steyadaṇḍaḥ kṛtabhāṇḍopadhau ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 27.1]

tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 29.1]
varṇotkarṣam apasāraṇaṃ yogaṃ vā sādhayataḥ pañcaśato daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 30.1]
tayor apacaraṇe rāgasyāpahāraṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 31.1]
māṣako vetanaṃ rūpyadharaṇasya suvarṇasyāṣṭabhāgaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 32.1]

tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 34.1]
tāmravṛttakaṃsavaikṛntakārakūṭakānāṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ vetanam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 35.1]

palahīne hīnadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 37.1]
tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 38.1]
sīsatrapupiṇḍo viṃśatibhāgakṣayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 39.1]

kālāyasapiṇḍaḥ pañcabhāgakṣayaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 41.1]

tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 43.1]
rūpadarśakasya sthitāṃ paṇayātrām akopyāṃ kopayataḥ kopyām akopayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 44.1]
vyājīpariśuddhau paṇayātrā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 45.1]
paṇān māṣakam upajīvato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 46.1]
tenottaraṃ vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 47.1]
kūṭarūpaṃ kārayataḥ pratigṛhṇato niryāpayato vā sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ kośe prakṣipato vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 48.1]
carakapāṃsudhāvakāḥ sāratribhāgaṃ labheran dvau rājā ratnaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 49.1]
ratnāpahāra uttamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 50.1]
khaniratnanidhinivedaneṣu ṣaṣṭham aṃśaṃ nivettā labheta dvādaśam aṃśaṃ bhṛtakaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 51.1]
śatasahasrād ūrdhvaṃ rājagāmī nidhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 52.1]
ūne ṣaṣṭham aṃśaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 53.1]
paurvapauruṣikaṃ nidhiṃ jānapadaḥ śuciḥ svakaraṇena samagraṃ labheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 54.1]
svakaraṇābhāve pañcaśato daṇḍaḥ pracchannādāne sahasram | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 55.1]
bhiṣajaḥ prāṇābādhikam anākhyāyopakramamāṇasya vipattau pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ karmāparādhena vipattau madhyamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 56.1]
marmavadhavaiguṇyakaraṇe daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 57.1]
kuśīlavā varṣārātram ekasthā vaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 58.1]
kāmadānam atimātram ekasyātivādaṃ ca varjayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 59.1]
tasyātikrame dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 60.1]
kāmaṃ deśajātigotracaraṇamaithunāvahāsena narmayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 61.1]

śeṣāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ niṣpattivetanaṃ śilpināṃ kalpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 64.1]

bhikṣukān kuhakāṃścānyān vārayed deśapīḍanāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 1 65.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 2}
saṃsthādhyakṣaḥ paṇyasaṃsthāyāṃ purāṇabhāṇḍānāṃ svakaraṇaviśuddhānām ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 1.1]
tulāmānabhāṇḍāni cāvekṣeta pautavāpacārāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 2.1]
parimāṇīdroṇayor ardhapalahīnātiriktam adoṣaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 3.1]
palahīnātirikte dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 4.1]
tena palottarā daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 5.1]
tulāyāḥ karṣahīnātiriktam adoṣaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 6.1]
dvikarṣahīnātirikte ṣaṭpaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 7.1]
tena karṣottarā daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 8.1]
āḍhakasyārdhakarṣahīnātiriktam adoṣaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 9.1]
karṣahīnātirikte tripaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 10.1]
tena karṣottarā daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 11.1]
tulāmānaviśeṣāṇām ato 'nyeṣām anumānaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 12.1]
tulāmānābhyām atiriktābhyāṃ krītvā hīnābhyāṃ vikrīṇānasya ta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 13.1]
gaṇyapaṇyeṣvaṣṭabhāgaṃ paṇyamūlyeṣvapaharataḥ ṣaṇṇavatir daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 14.1]
kāṣṭhalohamaṇimayaṃ rajjucarmamṛṇmayaṃ sūtravalkaromamayaṃ vā jātyam ityajātyaṃ vikrayādhānaṃ nayato mūlyāṣṭaguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 15.1]
sārabhāṇḍam ityasārabhāṇḍaṃ tajjātam ityatajjātaṃ rādhāyuktam ityupadhiyuktaṃ samudgaparivartimaṃ vā vikrayādhānaṃ nayato hīnamūlyaṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ paṇamūlyaṃ dviguṇo dvipaṇamūlyaṃ dviśataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 16.1]
tenārghavṛddhau daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 17.1]
kāruśilpināṃ karmaguṇāpakarṣam ājīvaṃ vikrayakrayopaghātaṃ vā sambhūya samutthāpayatāṃ sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 18.1]
vaidehakānāṃ vā sambhūya paṇyam avarundhatām anargheṇa vikrīṇatāṃ vā sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 19.1]
tulāmānāntaram arghavarṇāntaraṃ vā dharakasya māyakasya vā paṇamūlyād aṣṭabhāgaṃ hastadoṣeṇācarato dviśato daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 20.1]
tena dviśatottarā daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 21.1]
dhānyasnehakṣāralavaṇagandhabhaiṣajyadravyāṇāṃ samavarṇopadhāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 22.1]
yannisṛṣṭam upajīveyustad eṣāṃ divasasaṃjātaṃ saṃkhyāya vaṇik sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 23.1]
kretṛvikretror antarapatitam ādāyād anyad bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 24.1]
tena dhānyapaṇyanicayāṃścānujñātāḥ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 25.1]
anyathānicitam eṣāṃ paṇyādhyakṣo gṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 26.1]
tena dhānyapaṇyavikraye vyavaharetānugraheṇa prajānām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 27.1]
anujñātakrayād upari caiṣāṃ svadeśīyānāṃ paṇyānāṃ pañcakaṃ śatam ājīvaṃ sthāpayet paradeśīyānāṃ daśakam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 28.1]
tataḥ param arghaṃ vardhayatāṃ kraye vikraye vā bhāvayatāṃ paṇaśate pañcapaṇād dviśato daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 29.1]
tenārghavṛddhau daṇḍavṛddhir vyākhyātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 30.1]
sambhūyakraye caiṣām avikrīte nānyaṃ sambhūyakrayaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 31.1]
paṇyopaghāte caiṣām anugrahaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 32.1]
paṇyabāhulyāt paṇyādhyakṣaḥ sarvapaṇyānyekamukhāni vikrīṇīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 33.1]
teṣvavikrīteṣu nānye vikrīṇīran | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 34.1]
tāni divasavetanena vikrīṇīrann anugraheṇa prajānām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 35.1]
deśakālāntaritānāṃ tu paṇyānāṃ prakṣepaṃ paṇyaniṣpattiṃ śulkaṃ vṛddhim avakrayam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 36.1]
vyayān anyāṃśca saṃkhyāya sthāpayed argham arghavit | [ArthaŚ, 4, 2 36.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 3}
daivāni | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464887_1]
daivāni aṣṭau mahā bhayāni agniḥ udakam vyādhiḥ durbhikṣam mūṣikāḥ vyālāḥ sarpāḥ rakṣāṃsi iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464887_2]
tebhyaḥ janapadam rakṣet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464888_1]
grīṣme bahis adhiśrayaṇam grāmāḥ kuryuḥ saṃgraheṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464889_1]
nāgarika praṇidhau agni pratiṣedhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ niśānta praṇidhau rāja parigrahe ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464890_1]
bali homa svastivācanaiḥ parvasu ca agni pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464891_1]
varṣārātram ānūpa grāmāḥ pūra velām utsṛjya vaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464892_1]
kāṣṭhaveṇunāvaś copagṛhṇīyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 7.1]
uhyamānam alābu dṛti plava gaṇḍikā veṇikābhiḥ tārayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464894_1]
an abhisaratām dvādaśa paṇaḥ daṇḍaḥ anyatra plava hīnebhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464895_1]
parvasu ca nadī pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464896_1]
māyā yoga vidaḥ veda vidaḥ vā varṣam abhicareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464897_1]
varṣa avagrahe śacī nātha gaṅgā parvata mahā kaccha pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464898_1]
vyādhi bhayam aupaniṣadikaiḥ pratīkāraiḥ pratikuryuḥ auṣadhaiḥ cikitsakāḥ śānti prāyaścittaiḥ vā siddha tāpasāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464899_1]
tena marakaḥ vyākhyātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464900_1]
tīrtha abhiṣecanam mahā kaccha vardhanam gavām śmaśāna avadohanam kabandha dahanam deva rātrim ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464901_1]
paśu vyādhi marake sthāna artha nīrājanam sva daivata pūjanam ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464902_1]
durbhikṣe rājā bīja bhaktā upagraham kṛtvā anugraham kuryāt durga setu karma vā bhakta anugraheṇa bhakta saṃvibhāgam vā deśa nikṣepam vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464903_1]
mitrāṇi vā vyapāśrayeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464904_1]
karśanam vamanam vā kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464904_2]
niṣpanna sasyam anya viṣayam vā sa janapadaḥ yāyāt samudra saraḥ taṭākāni vā saṃśrayeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464905_1]
dhānya śāka mūla phala āvāpān vā setuṣu kurvīta mṛga paśu pakṣi vyāla matsya ārambhān vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464906_1]
mūṣika bhaye mārjāra nakula utsargaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464907_1]
teṣām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464908_1]
teṣām grahaṇa hiṃsāyām dvādaśa paṇaḥ daṇḍaḥ śunām anigrahe ca anyatra araṇya carebhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464908_2]
snuhi kṣīra liptāni dhānyāni visṛjet upaniṣad yoga yuktāni vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464909_1]
mūṣika karam vā prayuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464910_1]
śāntim vā siddha tāpasāḥ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464911_1]
parvasu ca mūṣika pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464912_1]
tena śalabha pakṣi krimi bhaya pratīkārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464913_1]
vyāla bhaye madana rasa yuktāni paśu śavāni prasṛjet madana kodrava pūrṇāni audaryāṇi vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464914_1]
lubdhakāḥ śva gaṇinaḥ vā kūṭa pañjara avapātaiḥ careyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464915_1]
āvaraṇinaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ vyālān abhihanyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464916_1]
an abhisartuḥ dvādaśa paṇaḥ daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464917_1]
saḥ eva lābhaḥ vyāla ghātinaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464918_1]
parvasu ca parvata pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464919_1]
tena mṛga paśu pakṣi saṃgha grāha pratīkārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464920_1]
sarpa bhaye mantraiḥ oṣadhibhiḥ ca jāṅgulī vidaḥ careyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464921_1]
sambhūya vā api sarpān hanyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464922_1]
atharvaveda vidaḥ vā abhicareyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464923_1]
parvasu ca nāga pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464924_1]
tena udaka prāṇi bhaya pratīkārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464925_1]
rakṣaḥ bhaye rakṣaḥ ghnāni atharvaveda vidaḥ māyā yoga vidaḥ vā karmāṇi kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464926_1]
parvasu ca vitardi chatra ullopikā hasta patākā chāga upahāraiḥ caitya pūjāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464927_1]
carum vaḥ carāmaḥ iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464928_1]
carum vaḥ carāmaḥ iti evam sarva bhayeṣu ahorātram careyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464928_2]
sarvatra ca upahatān pitā iva anugṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464929_1]
māyā yoga vidaḥ tasmāt viṣaye siddha tāpasāḥ vaseyuḥ pūjitāḥ rājñā daiva āpad pratikāriṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 3 464931_1]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 4}
samāhartṛpraṇidhau janapadarakṣaṇam uktam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 1.1]
tasya kaṇṭakaśodhanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 2.1]
samāhartā janapade siddhatāpasapravrajitacakracaracāraṇakuhakapracchandakakārtāntikanaimittikamauhūrtikacikitsakonmattamūkabadhirajaḍāndhavaidehakakāruśilpikuśīlavaveśaśauṇḍikāpūpikapākvamāṃsikaudanikavyañjanān praṇidadhyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 3.1]
te grāmāṇām adhyakṣāṇāṃ ca śaucāśaucaṃ vidyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 4.1]
yaṃ cātra gūḍhājīvinaṃ śaṅketa taṃ sattriṇāpasarpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 5.1]
dharmasthaṃ viśvāsopagataṃ sattrī brūyād asau me bandhur abhiyuktaḥ tasyāyam anarthaḥ pratikriyatām ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 6.1]
sa cet tathā kuryād upadāgrāhaka iti pravāsyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 7.1]
tena pradeṣṭāro vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 8.1]
grāmakūṭam adhyakṣaṃ vā sattrī brūyād asau jālmaḥ prabhūtadravyas tasyāyam anarthaḥ tenainam āhārayasva iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 9.1]
sa cet tathā kuryād utkocaka iti pravāsyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 10.1]
kṛtakābhiyukto vā kūṭasākṣiṇo 'bhijñātānarthavaipulyenārabheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 11.1]
te cet tathā kuryuḥ kūṭasākṣiṇa iti pravāsyeran | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 12.1]
tena kūṭaśrāvaṇakārakā vyākhyātāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 13.1]
yaṃ vā mantrayogamūlakarmabhiḥ śmāśānikair vā saṃvadanakārakaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī brūyād amuṣya bhāryāṃ snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ vā kāmaye sā māṃ pratikāmayatām ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 14.1]
sa cet tathā kuryāt saṃvadanakāraka iti pravāsyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 15.1]
tena kṛtyābhicāraśīlau vyākhyātau | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 16.1]
yaṃ vā rasasya kartāraṃ kretāraṃ vikretāraṃ bhaiṣajyāhāravyavahāriṇaṃ vā rasadaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī brūyād asau me śatruḥ tasyopaghātaḥ kriyatām ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 17.1]
sa cet tathā kuryād rasada iti pravāsyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 18.1]
tena madanayogavyavahārī vyākhyātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 19.1]
yaṃ vā nānālohakṣārāṇām aṅgārabhastrāsaṃdaṃśamuṣṭikādhikaraṇībimbaṭaṅkamūṣāṇām abhīkṣṇakretāraṃ maṣībhasmadhūmadigdhahastavastraliṅgaṃ karmāropakaraṇasaṃsargaṃ kūṭarūpakārakaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī śiṣyatvena saṃvyavahāreṇa cānupraviśya prajñāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 20.1]
prajñātaḥ kūṭarūpakāraka iti pravāsyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 21.1]
tena rāgasyāpahartā kūṭasuvarṇavyavahārī ca vyākhyātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 22.1]
ārabdhārastu hiṃsāyāṃ gūḍhājīvāstrayodaśa | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 23.1]
pravāsyā niṣkrayārthaṃ vā dadyur doṣaviśeṣataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 4 23.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 5}
sattriprayogād ūrdhvaṃ siddhavyañjanā māṇavān māṇavavidyābhiḥ pralobhayeyuḥ prasvāpanāntardhānadvārāpohamantreṇa pratirodhakān saṃvadanamantreṇa pāratalpikān | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 1.1]
teṣāṃ kṛtotsāhānāṃ mahāntaṃ saṃgham ādāya rātrāvanyaṃ grāmam uddiśyānyaṃ grāmaṃ kṛtakastrīpuruṣaṃ gatvā brūyuḥ ihaiva vidyāprabhāvo dṛśyatāṃ kṛcchraḥ paragrāmo gantum iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 2.1]
tato dvārāpohamantreṇa dvārāṇyapohya praviśyatām iti brūyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 3.1]
antardhānamantreṇa jāgratām ārakṣiṇāṃ madhyena māṇavān atikrāmayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 4.1]
prasvāpanamantreṇa prasvāpayitvā rakṣiṇaḥ śayābhir māṇavaiḥ saṃcārayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 5.1]
saṃvadanamantreṇa bhāryāvyañjanāḥ pareṣāṃ māṇavaiḥ saṃmodayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 6.1]
upalabdhavidyāprabhāvāṇāṃ puraścaraṇādyādiśeyur abhijñānārtham | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 7.1]
kṛtalakṣaṇadravyeṣu vā veśmasu karma kārayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 8.1]
anupraviṣṭā vaikatra grāhayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 9.1]
kṛtalakṣaṇadravyakrayavikrayādhāneṣu yogasurāmattān vā grāhayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 10.1]
gṛhītān pūrvāpadānasahāyān anuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 11.1]
purāṇacoravyañjanā vā corān anupraviṣṭāstathaiva karma kārayeyur grāhayeyuśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 12.1]
gṛhītān samāhartā paurajānapadānāṃ darśayet coragrahaṇīṃ vidyām adhīte rājā tasyopadeśād ime corā gṛhītāḥ bhūyaśca grahīṣyāmi vārayitavyo vaḥ svajanaḥ pāpācāra iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 13.1]
yaṃ cātrāpasarpopadeśena śamyāpratodādīnām apahartāraṃ jānīyāt tam eṣāṃ pratyādiśed eṣa rājñaḥ prabhāvaḥ iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 14.1]
purāṇacoragopālakavyādhaśvagaṇinaśca vanacorāṭavikān anupraviṣṭāḥ prabhūtakūṭahiraṇyakupyabhāṇḍeṣu sārthavrajagrāmeṣvenān abhiyojayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 15.1]
abhiyoge gūḍhabalair ghātayeyuḥ madanarasayuktena vā pathyadanena | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 16.1]
gṛhītaloptrabhārān āyatagatapariśrāntān prasvapataḥ prahavaṇeṣu yogasurāmattān vā grāhayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 17.1]
pūrvavacca gṛhītvainān samāhartā prarūpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 18.1]
sarvajñakhyāpanaṃ rājñaḥ kārayan rāṣṭravāsiṣu | [ArthaŚ, 4, 5 18.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 6}
siddhaprayogād ūrdhvaṃ śaṅkārūpakarmābhigrahaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 1.1]
kṣīṇadāyakuṭumbam alpanirveśaṃ viparītadeśajātigotranāmakarmāpadeśaṃ pracchannavṛttikarmāṇaṃ māṃsasurābhakṣyabhojanagandhamālyavastravibhūṣaṇeṣu prasaktam ativyayakartāraṃ puṃścalīdyūtaśauṇḍikeṣu prasaktam abhīkṣṇapravāsinam avijñātasthānagamanam ekāntāraṇyaniṣkuṭavikālacāriṇaṃ pracchanne sāmiṣe vā deśe bahumantrasaṃnipātaṃ sadyaḥkṣatavraṇānāṃ gūḍhapratīkārakārayitāram antargṛhanityam abhyadhigantāraṃ kāntāparaṃ paraparigrahāṇāṃ parastrīdravyaveśmanām abhīkṣṇapraṣṭāraṃ kutsitakarmaśāstropakaraṇasaṃsargaṃ virātre channakuḍyacchāyāsaṃcāriṇaṃ virūpadravyāṇām adeśakālavikretāraṃ jātavairāśayaṃ hīnakarmajātiṃ vigūhamānarūpaṃ liṅgenāliṅginaṃ liṅginaṃ vā bhinnācāraṃ pūrvakṛtāpadānaṃ svakarmabhir apadiṣṭaṃ nāgarikamahāmātradarśane gūhamānam apasarantam anucchvāsopaveśinam āvignaṃ śuṣkabhinnasvaramukhavarṇaṃ śastrahastamanuṣyasampātatrāsinaṃ hiṃsrastenanidhinikṣepāpahāraparaprayogagūḍhājīvinām anyatamaṃ śaṅketa | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 2.1]
iti śaṅkābhigrahaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 3.1]
rūpābhigrahastu naṣṭāpahṛtam avidyamānaṃ tajjātavyavahāriṣu nivedayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 4.1]
taccen niveditam āsādya pracchādayeyuḥ sācivyakaradoṣam āpnuyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 5.1]
ajānanto 'sya dravyasyātisargeṇa mucyeran | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 6.1]
na cānivedya saṃsthādhyakṣasya purāṇabhāṇḍānām ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 7.1]
taccen niveditam āsādyeta rūpābhigṛhītam āgamaṃ pṛcchet kutaste labdham iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 8.1]
sa cet brūyāt dāyādyād avāptam amuṣmāllabdhaṃ krītaṃ kāritam ādhipracchannam ayam asya deśaḥ kālaścopasamprāpter ayam asyārghaḥ pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mūlyaṃ ca iti tasyāgamasamādhau mucyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 9.1]
nāṣṭikaścet tad eva pratisaṃdadhyād yasya pūrvo dīrghaśca paribhogaḥ śucir vā deśas tasya dravyam iti vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 10.1]
catuṣpadadvipadānām api hi rūpaliṅgasāmānyaṃ bhavati kim aṅga punar ekayonidravyakartṛprasūtānāṃ kupyābharaṇabhāṇḍānām iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 11.1]
sa ced brūyāt yācitakam avakrītakam āhitakaṃ nikṣepam upanidhiṃ vaiyāvṛtyakarma vāmuṣya iti tasyāpasārapratisaṃdhānena mucyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 12.1]
naivam ityapasāro vā brūyād rūpābhigṛhītaḥ parasya dānakāraṇam ātmanaḥ pratigrahakāraṇam upaliṅganaṃ vā dāyakadāpakanibandhakapratigrāhakopadraṣṭṛbhir upaśrotṛbhir vā pratisamānayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 13.1]
ujhitapranaṣṭaniṣpatitopalabdhasya deśakālalābhopaliṅganena śuddhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 14.1]
aśuddhastacca tāvacca daṇḍaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 15.1]
anyathā steyadaṇḍaṃ bhajeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 16.1]
iti rūpābhigrahaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 17.1]
karmābhigrahastu muṣitaveśmanaḥ praveśaniṣkasanam advāreṇa dvārasya saṃdhinā bījena vā vedham uttamāgārasya jālavātāyananīpravedham ārohaṇāvataraṇe ca kuḍyasya vedham upakhananaṃ vā gūḍhadravyanikṣepaṇagrahaṇopāyam upadeśopalabhyam abhyantaracchedotkaraparimardopakaraṇam abhyantarakṛtaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 17.2]
viparyaye bāhyakṛtam ubhayata ubhayakṛtam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 18.1]
abhyantarakṛte puruṣam āsannaṃ vyasaninaṃ krūrasahāyaṃ taskaropakaraṇasaṃsargaṃ striyaṃ vā daridrakulām anyaprasaktāṃ vā paricārakajanaṃ vā tadvidhācāram atisvapnaṃ nidrāklāntam āvignaṃ śuṣkabhinnasvaramukhavarṇam anavasthitam atipralāpinam uccārohaṇasaṃrabdhagātraṃ vilūnanighṛṣṭabhinnapāṭitaśarīravastraṃ jātakiṇasaṃrabdhahastapādaṃ pāṃsupūrṇakeśanakhaṃ vilūnabhugnakeśanakhaṃ vā samyaksnātānuliptaṃ tailapramṛṣṭagātraṃ sadyodhautahastapādaṃ vā pāṃsupicchileṣu tulyapādapadanikṣepaṃ praveśaniṣkasanayor vā tulyamālyamadyagandhavastracchedavilepanasvedaṃ parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 19.1]
coraṃ pāradārikaṃ vā vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 20.1]
sagopasthāniko bāhyaṃ pradeṣṭā coramārgaṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 21.1]
kuryān nāgarikaścāntardurge nirdiṣṭahetubhiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 6 21.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 7}
tailābhyaktam āśumṛtakaṃ parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 1.1]
niṣkīrṇamūtrapurīṣaṃ vātapūrṇakoṣṭhatvakkaṃ śūnapādapāṇim unmīlitākṣaṃ savyañjanakaṇṭhaṃ pīḍananiruddhocchvāsahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 2.1]
tam eva saṃkucitabāhusakthim udbandhahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 3.1]
śūnapāṇipādodaram apagatākṣam udvṛttanābhim avaropitaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 4.1]
nistabdhagudākṣaṃ saṃdaṣṭajihvam ādhmātodaram udakahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 5.1]
śoṇitānusiktaṃ bhagnabhinnagātraṃ kāṣṭhair aśmabhir vā hataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 6.1]
saṃbhagnasphuṭitagātram avakṣiptaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 7.1]
śyāvapāṇipādadantanakhaṃ śithilamāṃsaromacarmāṇaṃ phenopadigdhamukhaṃ viṣahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 8.1]
tam eva saśoṇitadaṃśaṃ sarpakīṭahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 9.1]
vikṣiptavastragātram ativāntaviriktaṃ madanayogahataṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 9.2]
ato 'nyatamena kāraṇena hataṃ hatvā vā daṇḍabhayād udbaddhanikṛttakaṇṭhaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 10.1]
viṣahatasya bhojanaśeṣaṃ vayobhiḥ parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 11.1]
hṛdayād uddhṛtyāgnau prakṣiptaṃ ciṭiciṭāyadindradhanurvarṇaṃ vā viṣayuktaṃ vidyāt dagdhasya hṛdayam adagdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 12.1]
tasya paricārakajanaṃ vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyātilabdhaṃ mārgeta duḥkhopahatam anyaprasaktaṃ vā strījanaṃ dāyavṛttistrījanābhimantāraṃ vā bandhum | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 13.1]
tad eva hatodbaddhasya parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 14.1]
svayam udbaddhasya vā viprakāram ayuktaṃ mārgeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 15.1]
sarveṣāṃ vā strīdāyādyadoṣaḥ karmaspardhā pratipakṣadveṣaḥ paṇyasaṃsthāsamavāyo vā vivādapadānām anyatamad vā roṣasthānam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 16.1]
roṣanimitto ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 17.1]
svayamādiṣṭapuruṣair vā corair arthanimittaṃ sādṛśyād anyavairibhir vā hatasya ghātam āsannebhyaḥ parīkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 18.1]
yenāhūtaḥ saha sthitaḥ prasthito hatabhūmim ānīto vā tam anuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 19.1]
ye cāsya hatabhūmāvāsannacarās tān ekaikaśaḥ pṛcchet kenāyam ihānīto hato vā kaḥ saśastraḥ saṃgūhamāna udvigno vā yuṣmābhir dṛṣṭaḥ iti | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 20.1]
te yathā brūyustathānuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 21.1]
anāthasya śarīrastham upabhogaṃ paricchadam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 22.1]
vastraṃ veṣaṃ vibhūṣāṃ vā dṛṣṭvā tadvyavahāriṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 22.2]
anuyuñjīta saṃyogaṃ nivāsaṃ vāsakāraṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 23.1]
karma ca vyavahāraṃ ca tato mārgaṇam ācaret | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 23.2]
rajjuśastraviṣair vāpi kāmakrodhavaśena yaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 24.1]
ghātayet svayam ātmānaṃ strī vā pāpena mohitā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 24.2]
rajjunā rājamārge tāṃścaṇḍālenāpakarṣayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 25.1]
na śmaśānavidhisteṣāṃ na sambandhikriyāstathā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 25.2]
bandhusteṣāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pretakāryakriyāvidhim | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 26.1]
tadgatiṃ sa caret paścāt svajanād vā pramucyate | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 26.2]
saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena samācaran | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 27.1]
yājanādhyāpanād yaunāt taiścānyo 'pi samācaran | [ArthaŚ, 4, 7 27.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 8}
muṣitasaṃnidhau bāhyānām abhyantarāṇāṃ ca sākṣiṇām abhiśastasya deśajātigotranāmakarmasārasahāyanivāsān anuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 1.1]
tāṃścāpadeśaiḥ pratisamānayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 2.1]
tataḥ pūrvasyāhnaḥ pracāraṃ rātrau nivāsaṃ ca grahaṇād ityanuyuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 3.1]
tasyāpasārapratisaṃdhāne śuddhaḥ syāt anyathā karmaprāptaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 4.1]
trirātrād ūrdhvam agrāhyaḥ śaṅkitakaḥ pṛcchābhāvād anyatropakaraṇadarśanāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 5.1]
acoraṃ cora ityabhivyāharataścorasamo daṇḍaś coraṃ pracchādayataśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 6.1]
coreṇābhiśasto vairadveṣābhyām apadiṣṭakaḥ śuddhaḥ syāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 7.1]
śuddhaṃ parivāsayataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 8.1]
śaṅkāniṣpannam upakaraṇamantrisahāyarūpavaiyāvṛtyakarān niṣpādayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 9.1]
karmaṇaśca pradeśadravyādānāṃśavibhāgaiḥ pratisamānayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 10.1]
eteṣāṃ kāraṇānām anabhisaṃdhāne vipralapantam acoraṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 11.1]
dṛśyate hyacoro 'pi coramārge yadṛcchayā saṃnipāte coraveṣaśastrabhāṇḍasāmānyena gṛhyamāṇaścorabhāṇḍasyopavāsena vā yathāṇimāṇḍavyaḥ karmakleśabhayād acoraḥ coro 'smi iti bruvāṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 12.1]
tasmāt samāptakaraṇaṃ niyamayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 13.1]
mandāparādhaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ vyādhitaṃ mattam unmattaṃ kṣutpipāsādhvaklāntam atyāśitam āmakāśitaṃ durbalaṃ vā na karma kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 14.1]
tulyaśīlapuṃścalīprāpāvikakathāvakāśabhojanadātṛbhir apasarpayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 15.1]
evam atisaṃdadhyād yathā vā nikṣepāpahāre vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 16.1]
āptadoṣaṃ karma kārayenna tveva striyaṃ garbhiṇīṃ sūtikāṃ vā māsāvaraprajātām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 17.1]
striyāstvardhakarma vākyānuyogo vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 18.1]
brāhmaṇasya sattriparigrahaḥ śrutavatastapasvinaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 19.1]
tasyātikrama uttamo daṇḍaḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca karmaṇā vyāpādanena ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 20.1]
vyāvahārikaṃ karmacatuṣkaṃ ṣaḍ daṇḍāḥ sapta kaśāḥ dvāv uparinibandhau udakanālikā ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 21.1]
paraṃ pāpakarmaṇāṃ nava vetralatāḥ dvādaśa kaśāḥ dvāv ūruveṣṭau viṃśatir naktamālalatāḥ dvātriṃśattalāḥ dvau vṛścikabandhau ullambane ca dve sūcī hastasya yavāgūpītasya ekaparvadahanam aṅgulyāḥ snehapītasya pratāpanam ekam ahaḥ śiśirarātrau balbajāgraśayyā ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 22.1]
ityaṣṭādaśakaṃ karma | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 23.1]
tasyopakaraṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ praharaṇaṃ pradhāraṇam avadhāraṇaṃ ca kharapaṭṭād āgamayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 24.1]
divasāntaram ekaikaṃ ca karma kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 25.1]
pūrvakṛtāpadānaṃ pratijñāyāpaharantam ekadeśadṛṣṭadravyaṃ karmaṇā rūpeṇa vā gṛhītaṃ rājakośam avastṛṇantaṃ karmavadhyaṃ vā rājavacanāt samastaṃ vyastam abhyastaṃ vā karma kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 26.1]
sarvāparādheṣvapīḍanīyo brāhmaṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 27.1]
tasyābhiśastāṅko lalāṭe syād vyavahārapatanāya steye śvā manuṣyavadhe kabandho gurutalpe bhagaṃ surāpāne madyadhvajaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 28.1]
brāhmaṇaṃ pāpakarmāṇam udghuṣyāṅkakṛtavraṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 29.1]
kuryān nirviṣayaṃ rājā vāsayed ākareṣu vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 8 29.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 9}
samāhartṛpradeṣṭāraḥ pūrvam adhyakṣāṇām adhyakṣapuruṣāṇāṃ ca niyamanaṃ kuryuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 1.1]
khanisārakarmāntebhyaḥ sāraṃ ratnaṃ vāpaharataḥ śuddhavadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 2.1]
phalgudravyakarmāntebhyaḥ phalgu dravyam upaskaraṃ vā pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 3.1]
paṇyabhūmibhyo vā rājapaṇyaṃ māṣamūlyād ūrdhvam ā pādamūlyād ityapaharato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ ā dvipādamūlyād iti caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ ā tripādamūlyād iti ṣaṭtriṃśatpaṇaḥ ā paṇamūlyād ityaṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ ā dvipaṇamūlyād iti pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ ā catuṣpaṇamūlyād iti madhyamaḥ āṣṭapaṇamūlyād ityuttamaḥ ā daśapaṇamūlyād iti vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 4.1]
koṣṭhapaṇyakupyāyudhāgārebhyaḥ kupyabhāṇḍopaskarāpahāreṣvardhamūlyeṣu eta eva daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 5.1]
kośabhāṇḍāgārākṣaśālābhyaś caturbhāgamūlyeṣu eta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 6.1]
corāṇām abhipradharṣaṇe citro ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 7.1]
iti rājaparigraheṣu vyākhyātam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 8.1]
bāhyeṣu tu pracchannam ahani kṣetrakhalaveśmāpaṇebhyaḥ kupyabhāṇḍam upaskaraṃ vā māṣamūlyād ūrdhvam ā pādamūlyād ityapaharatastripaṇo daṇḍaḥ gomayapradehena vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇam ā dvipādamūlyād iti ṣaṭpaṇaḥ gomayabhasmanā vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇam ā tripādamūlyād iti navapaṇaḥ gomayabhasmanā vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇam śarāvamekhalayā vā ā paṇamūlyād iti dvādaśapaṇaḥ muṇḍanaṃ pravrājanaṃ vā ā dvipaṇamūlyād iti caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ muṇḍasyeṣṭakāśakalena pravrājanaṃ vā ā catuṣpaṇamūlyād iti ṣaṭtriṃśatpaṇa ā pañcapaṇamūlyād ityaṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ ā daśapaṇamūlyād iti pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍa ā viṃśatipaṇamūlyād iti dviśata ā triṃśatpaṇamūlyād iti pañcaśata ā catvāriṃśatpaṇamūlyād iti sāhasra ā pañcāśatpaṇamūlyād iti vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 9.1]
prasahya divā rātrau vāntaryāmikam apaharato 'rdhamūlyeṣu eta eva daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 10.1]
prasahya divā rātrau vā saśastrasyāpaharataścaturbhāgamūlyeṣu eta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 11.1]
kuṭuṃbikādhyakṣamukhyasvāmināṃ kūṭaśāsanamudrākarmasu pūrvamadhyottamavadhā daṇḍāḥ yathāparādhaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 12.1]
dharmasthaśced vivadamānaṃ puruṣaṃ tarjayati bhartsayatyapasārayatyabhigrasate vā pūrvam asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt vākpāruṣye dviguṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 13.1]
pṛcchyaṃ na pṛcchati apṛcchyaṃ pṛcchati pṛṣṭvā vā visṛjati śikṣayati smārayati pūrvaṃ dadāti vā iti madhyamam asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 14.1]
deyaṃ deśaṃ na pṛcchati adeyaṃ deśaṃ pṛcchati kāryam adeśenātivāhayati chalenātiharati kālaharaṇena śrāntam apavāhayati mārgāpannaṃ vākyam utkramayati matisāhāyyaṃ sākṣibhyo dadāti tāritānuśiṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ punar api gṛhṇāti uttamam asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 15.1]
punaraparādhe dviguṇaṃ sthānād vyavaropaṇaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 16.1]
lekhakaśced uktaṃ na likhati anuktaṃ likhati duruktam upalikhati sūktam ullikhati arthotpattiṃ vā vikalpayati iti pūrvam asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryād yathāparādhaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 17.1]
dharmasthaḥ pradeṣṭā vā hairaṇyadaṇḍam adaṇḍye kṣipati kṣepadviguṇam asmai daṇḍaṃ kuryāt hīnātiriktāṣṭaguṇaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 18.1]
śarīradaṇḍaṃ kṣipati śārīram eva daṇḍaṃ bhajeta niṣkrayadviguṇaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 19.1]
yaṃ vā bhūtam arthaṃ nāśayati abhūtam arthaṃ karoti tadaṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 20.1]
dharmasthīye cārake bandhanāgāre vā śayyāsanabhojanoccārasaṃcārarodhabandhaneṣu tripaṇottarā daṇḍāḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 21.1]
cārakād abhiyuktaṃ muñcato niṣpātayato vā madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ abhiyogadānaṃ ca bandhanāgārāt sarvasvaṃ vadhaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 22.1]
bandhanāgārādhyakṣasya saṃruddhakam anākhyāya cārayataścaturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ karma kārayato dviguṇaḥ sthānānyatvaṃ gamayato 'nnapānaṃ vā rundhataḥ ṣaṇṇavatir daṇḍaḥ parikleśayata utkoṭayato vā madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ ghnataḥ sāhasraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 23.1]
parigṛhītāṃ dāsīm āhitikāṃ vā saṃruddhikām adhicarataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaś coraḍāmarikabhāryāṃ madhyamaḥ saṃruddhikām āryām uttamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 24.1]
saṃruddhasya vā tatraiva ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 25.1]
tad evākṣaṇagṛhītāyām āryāyāṃ vidyād dāsyāṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 26.1]
cārakam abhittvā niṣpātayato madhyamaḥ bhittvā vadhaḥ bandhanāgārāt sarvasvaṃ vadhaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 27.1]
evam arthacarān pūrvaṃ rājā daṇḍena śodhayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 28.1]
śodhayeyuśca śuddhāste paurajānapadān damaiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 9 28.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 10}
tīrthaghātagranthibhedordhvakarāṇāṃ prathame 'parādhe saṃdeśacchedanaṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo vā daṇḍaḥ dvitīye chedanaṃ paṇasya śatyo vā daṇḍas tṛtīye dakṣiṇahastavadhaścatuḥśato vā daṇḍaś caturthe yathākāmī vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 1.1]
pañcaviṃśatipaṇāvareṣu kukkuṭanakulamārjāraśvasūkarasteyeṣu hiṃsāyāṃ vā catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍo nāsāgracchedanaṃ vā caṇḍālāraṇyacarāṇām ardhadaṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 2.1]
pāśajālakūṭāvapāteṣu baddhānāṃ mṛgapaśupakṣivyālamatsyānām ādāne tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 3.1]
mṛgadravyavanān mṛgadravyāpahāre śatyo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 4.1]
biṃbavihāramṛgapakṣisteye hiṃsāyāṃ vā dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 5.1]
kāruśilpikuśīlavatapasvināṃ kṣudrakadravyāpahāre śatyo daṇḍaḥ sthūlakadravyāpahāre dviśataḥ kṛṣidravyāpahāre ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 6.1]
durgam akṛtapraveśasya praviśataḥ prākāracchidrād vā nikṣepaṃ gṛhītvāpasarataḥ kāṇḍarāvadho dviśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 7.1]
cakrayuktaṃ nāvaṃ kṣudrapaśuṃ vāpaharata ekapādavadhaḥ triśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 8.1]
kūṭakākaṇyakṣārālāśalākāhastaviṣamakāriṇa ekahastavadhaḥ catuḥśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 9.1]
stenapāradārikayoḥ sācivyakarmaṇi striyāḥ saṃgṛhītāyāśca karṇanāsāchedanaṃ pañcaśato vā daṇḍaḥ puṃso dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 10.1]
mahāpaśum ekaṃ dāsaṃ dāsīṃ vāpaharataḥ pretabhāṇḍaṃ vā vikrīṇānasya dvipādavadhaḥ ṣaṭchato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 11.1]
varṇottamānāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca hastapādalaṅghane rājayānavāhanādyārohaṇe caikahastapādavadhaḥ saptaśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 12.1]
śūdrasya brāhmaṇavādino devadravyam avastṛṇato rājadviṣṭam ādiśato dvinetrabhedinaśca yogāñjanenāndhatvam aṣṭaśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 13.1]
coraṃ pāradārikaṃ vā mokṣayato rājaśāsanam ūnam atiriktaṃ vā likhataḥ kanyāṃ dāsīṃ vā sahiraṇyam apaharataḥ kūṭavyavahāriṇo vimāṃsavikrayiṇaśca vāmahastadvipādavadho navaśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 14.1]
mānuṣamāṃsavikraye vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 15.1]
devapaśupratimāmanuṣyakṣetragṛhahiraṇyasuvarṇaratnasasyāpahāriṇa uttamo daṇḍaḥ śuddhavadho vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 16.1]
puruṣaṃ cāparādhaṃ ca kāraṇaṃ gurulāghavam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 17.1]
anubandhaṃ tadātvaṃ ca deśakālau samīkṣya ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 17.2]
uttamāvaramadhyatvaṃ pradeṣṭā daṇḍakarmaṇi | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 18.1]
rājñaśca prakṛtīnāṃ ca kalpayed antarā sthitaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 10 18.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 11}
kalahe ghnataḥ puruṣaṃ citro ghātaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 1.1]
saptarātrasyāntarmṛte śuddhavadhaḥ pakṣasyāntar uttamo māsasyāntaḥ pañcaśataḥ samutthānavyayaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 2.1]
śastreṇa praharata uttamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 3.1]
madena hastavadhaḥ mohena dviśataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 4.1]
vadhe vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 5.1]
prahāreṇa garbhaṃ pātayata uttamo daṇḍo bhaiṣajyena madhyamaḥ parikleśena pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 6.1]
prasabhastrīpuruṣaghātakābhisārakanigrāhakāvaghoṣakāvaskandakopavedhakān pathiveśmapratirodhakān rājahastyaśvarathānāṃ hiṃsakān stenān vā śūlān ārohayeyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 7.1]
yaścainān dahed apanayed vā sa tam eva daṇḍaṃ labheta sāhasam uttamaṃ vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 8.1]
hiṃsrastenānāṃ bhaktavāsopakaraṇāgnimantradānavaiyāvṛtyakarmasūttamo daṇḍaḥ paribhāṣaṇam avijñāte | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 9.1]
hiṃsrastenānāṃ putradāram asamantraṃ visṛjet samantram ādadīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 10.1]
rājyakāmukam antaḥpurapradharṣakam aṭavyamitrotsāhakaṃ durgarāṣṭradaṇḍakopakaṃ vā śirohastapradīpikaṃ ghātayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 11.1]
brāhmaṇaṃ tamaḥ praveśayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 12.1]
mātṛpitṛputrabhrātrācāryatapasvighātakaṃ vātvakśiraḥpradīpikaṃ ghātayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 13.1]
teṣām ākrośe jihvāchedo 'ṅgābhiradane tadaṅgān mocyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 14.1]
yadṛcchāghāte puṃsaḥ paśuyūthasteye ca śuddhavadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 15.1]
daśāvaraṃ ca yūthaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 16.1]
udakadhāraṇaṃ setuṃ bhindatastatraivāpsu nimajjanam anudakam uttamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ bhagnotsṛṣṭakaṃ madhyamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 17.1]
viṣadāyakaṃ puruṣaṃ striyaṃ ca puruṣaghnīm apaḥ praveśayed agarbhiṇīm garbhiṇīṃ māsāvaraprajātām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 18.1]
patiguruprajāghātikām agniviṣadāṃ saṃdhichedikāṃ vā gobhiḥ pāṭayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 19.1]
vivītakṣetrakhalaveśmadravyahastivanādīpikam agninā dāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 20.1]
rājākrośakamantrabhedakayor aniṣṭapravṛttikasya brāhmaṇamahānasāvalehinaśca jihvām utpāṭayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 21.1]
praharaṇāvaraṇastenam anāyudhīyam iṣubhir ghātayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 22.1]
āyudhīyasyottamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 23.1]
meḍhraphalopaghātinastad eva chedayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 24.1]
jihvānāsopaghāte saṃdaṃśavadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 25.1]
ete śāstreṣvanugatāḥ kleśadaṇḍā mahātmanām | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 26.1]
akliṣṭānāṃ tu pāpānāṃ dharmyaḥ śuddhavadhaḥ smṛtaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 11 26.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 12}
savarṇām aprāptaphalāṃ prakurvato hastavadhaḥ catuḥśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 1.1]
mṛtāyāṃ vadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 2.1]
prāptaphalāṃ prakurvato madhyamāpradeśinīvadho dviśato vā daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 3.1]
pituścāvahīnaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 4.1]
na ca prākāmyam akāmāyāṃ labheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 5.1]
sakāmāyāṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ striyāstvardhadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 6.1]
paraśulkāvaruddhāyāṃ hastavadhaḥ catuḥśato vā daṇḍaḥ śulkadānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 7.1]
saptārtavaprajātāṃ varaṇād ūrdhvam alabhamānaḥ prakṛtya prākāmī syānna ca pitur avahīnaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 8.1]
ṛtupratirodhibhiḥ svāmyād apakrāmati | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 9.1]
trivarṣaprajātārtavāyāstulyo gantum adoṣas tataḥ param atulyo 'pyanalaṃkṛtāyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 10.1]
pitṛdravyādāne steyaṃ bhajeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 11.1]
param uddiśyānyasya vindato dviśato daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 12.1]
na ca prākāmyam akāmāyāṃ labheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 13.1]
kanyām anyāṃ darśayitvānyāṃ prayacchataḥ śatyo daṇḍastulyāyām hīnāyāṃ dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 14.1]
prakarmaṇy akumāryāś catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ śulkavyayakarmaṇī ca pratidadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 15.1]
avasthāya tajjātaṃ paścātkṛtā dviguṇaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 16.1]
anyaśoṇitopadhāne dviśato daṇḍo mithyābhiśaṃsinaśca puṃsaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 17.1]
śulkavyayakarmaṇī ca jīyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 18.1]
na ca prākāmyam akāmāyāṃ labheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 19.1]
strīprakṛtā sakāmā samānā dvādaśapaṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt prakartrī dviguṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 20.1]
akāmāyāḥ śatyo daṇḍa ātmarāgārtham śulkadānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 21.1]
svayaṃ prakṛtā rājadāsyaṃ gacchet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 22.1]
bahirgrāmasya prakṛtāyāṃ mithyābhiśaṃsane ca dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 23.1]
prasahya kanyām apaharato dviśataḥ sasuvarṇām uttamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 24.1]
bahūnāṃ kanyāpahāriṇāṃ pṛthag yathoktā daṇḍāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 25.1]
gaṇikāduhitaraṃ prakurvataścatuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ śulkaṃ mātur bhogaḥ ṣoḍaśaguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 26.1]
dāsasya dāsyā vā duhitaram adāsīṃ prakurvataścaturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ śulkāvandhyadānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 27.1]
niṣkrayānurūpāṃ dāsīṃ prakurvato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍo vastrāvandhyadānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 28.1]
sācivyāvakāśadāne kartṛsamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 29.1]
proṣitapatikām apacarantīṃ patibandhustatpuruṣo vā saṃgṛhṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 30.1]
saṃgṛhītā patim ākāṅkṣeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 31.1]
patiścet kṣameta visṛjyetobhayam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 32.1]
akṣamāyāṃ striyāḥ karṇanāsāchedanaṃ vadhaṃ jāraśca prāpnuyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 33.1]
jāraṃ cora ityabhiharataḥ pañcaśato daṇḍo hiraṇyena muñcatastadaṣṭaguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 34.1]
keśākeśikaṃ saṃgrahaṇam upaliṅganād vā śarīropabhogānām tajjātebhyaḥ strīvacanād vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 35.1]
paracakrāṭavīhṛtām oghapravyūḍhām araṇyeṣu durbhikṣe vā tyaktāṃ pretabhāvotsṛṣṭāṃ vā parastriyaṃ nistārayitvā yathāsaṃbhāṣitaṃ samupabhuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 36.1]
jātiviśiṣṭām akāmām apatyavatīṃ niṣkrayeṇa dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 37.1]
corahastānnadīvegād durbhikṣād deśavibhramāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 38.1]
nistārayitvā kāntārān naṣṭāṃ tyaktāṃ mṛteti vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 38.2]
bhuñjīta striyam anyeṣāṃ yathāsaṃbhāṣitaṃ naraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 39.1]
na tu rājapratāpena pramuktāṃ svajanena vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 39.2]
na cottamāṃ na cākāmāṃ pūrvāpatyavatīṃ na ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 40.1]
īdṛśīṃ tvanurūpeṇa niṣkrayeṇāpavāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 12 40.2]
{ArthaŚ, 4, 13}
brāhmaṇam apeyam abhakṣyaṃ vā grāsayata uttamo daṇḍaḥ kṣatriyaṃ madhyamaḥ vaiśyaṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ śūdraṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 1.1]
svayaṃ grasitāro nirviṣayāḥ kāryāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 2.1]
paragṛhābhigamane divā pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍo rātrau madhyamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 3.1]
divā rātrau vā saśastrasya praviśata uttamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 4.1]
bhikṣukavaidehakau mattonmattau balād āpadi cātisaṃnikṛṣṭāḥ pravṛttapraveśāś cādaṇḍyāḥ anyatra pratiṣedhāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 5.1]
svaveśmano virātrād ūrdhvaṃ parivāram ārohataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ paraveśmano madhyamaḥ grāmārāmavāṭabhedinaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 6.1]
grāmeṣvantaḥ sārthikā jñātasārā vaseyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 7.1]
muṣitaṃ pravāsitaṃ caiṣām anirgataṃ rātrau grāmasvāmī dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 8.1]
grāmāntareṣu vā muṣitaṃ pravāsitaṃ vivītādhyakṣo dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 9.1]
avivītānāṃ corarajjukaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 10.1]
tathāpyaguptānāṃ sīmāvarodhena vicayaṃ dadyuḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 11.1]
asīmāvarodhe pañcagrāmī daśagrāmī vā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 12.1]
durbalaṃ veśma śakaṭam anuttabdhamūrdhastaṃbhaṃ śastram anapāśrayam apraticchannaṃ śvabhraṃ kūpaṃ kūṭāvapātaṃ vā kṛtvā hiṃsāyāṃ daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ vidyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 13.1]
vṛkṣacchedane damyaraśmiharaṇe catuṣpadānām adāntasevane vāhane vā kāṣṭhaloṣṭapāṣāṇadaṇḍabāṇabāhuvikṣepaṇeṣu yāne hastinā ca saṃghaṭṭane apehi iti prakrośann adaṇḍyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 14.1]
hastinā roṣitena hato droṇānnaṃ madyakuṃbhaṃ mālyānulepanaṃ dantapramārjanaṃ ca paṭaṃ dadyāt | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 15.1]
aśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānena tulyo hastinā vadha iti pādaprakṣālanam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 16.1]
udāsīnavadhe yātur uttamo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 17.1]
śṛṅgiṇā daṃṣṭriṇā vā hiṃsyamānam amokṣayataḥ svāminaḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ pratikruṣṭasya dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 18.1]
śṛṅgidaṃṣṭribhyām anyonyaṃ ghātayatastacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 19.1]
devapaśum ṛṣabham ukṣāṇaṃ gokumārīṃ vā vāhayataḥ pañcaśato daṇḍaḥ pravāsayata uttamaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 20.1]
lomadohavāhanaprajananopakāriṇāṃ kṣudrapaśūnām ādāne tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ pravāsane ca anyatra devapitṛkāryebhyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 21.1]
chinnanasyaṃ bhagnayugaṃ tiryakpratimukhāgataṃ pratyāsarad vā cakrayuktaṃ yātā paśumanuṣyasaṃbādhe vā hiṃsāyām adaṇḍyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 22.1]
anyathā yathoktaṃ mānuṣaprāṇihiṃsāyāṃ daṇḍam abhyāvahet | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 23.1]
amānuṣaprāṇivadhe prāṇidānaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 24.1]
bāle yātari yānasthaḥ svāmī daṇḍyo 'svāmini yānasthaḥ prāptavyavahāro vā yātā | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 25.1]
bālādhiṣṭhitam apuruṣaṃ vā yānaṃ rājā haret | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 26.1]
kṛtyābhicārābhyāṃ yatparam āpādayet tadāpādayitavyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 27.1]
kāmaṃ bhāryāyām anicchantyāṃ kanyāyāṃ vā dārārthino bhartari bhāryāyā vā saṃvadanakaraṇam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 28.1]
anyathāhiṃsāyāṃ madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 29.1]
mātāpitror bhaginīṃ mātulānīm ācāryāṇīṃ snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ bhaginīṃ vādhicaratastriliṅgacchedanaṃ vadhaśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 30.1]
sakāmā tad eva labheta dāsaparicārakāhitakabhuktā ca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 31.1]
brāhmaṇyām aguptāyāṃ kṣatriyasyottamaḥ sarvasvaṃ vaiśyasya śūdraḥ kaṭāgninā dahyeta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 32.1]
sarvatra rājabhāryāgamane kumbhīpākaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 33.1]
śvapākīgamane kṛtakabandhāṅkaḥ paraviṣayaṃ gacchet śvapākatvaṃ vā śūdraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 34.1]
śvapākasyāryāgamane vadhaḥ striyāḥ karṇanāsāchedanam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 35.1]
pravrajitāgamane caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 36.1]
sakāmā tad eva labheta | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 37.1]
rūpājīvāyāḥ prasahyopabhoge dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 38.1]
bahūnām ekām adhicaratāṃ pṛthak caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 39.1]
striyam ayonau gacchataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ puruṣam adhimehataśca | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 40.1]
maithune dvādaśapaṇastiryagyoniṣvanātmanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 41.1]
daivatapratimānāṃ ca gamane dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 41.2]
adaṇḍyadaṇḍane rājño daṇḍastriṃśadguṇo 'mbhasi | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 42.1]
varuṇāya pradātavyo brāhmaṇebhyastataḥ param | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 42.2]
tena tat pūyate pāpaṃ rājño daṇḍāpacārajam | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 43.1]
śāstā hi varuṇo rājñāṃ mithyā vyācaratāṃ nṛṣu | [ArthaŚ, 4, 13 43.2]
{ArthaŚ, 10, 1}
vāstukapraśaste vāstuni nāyakavardhakimauhūrtikāḥ skandhāvāram vṛttaṃ dīrghaṃ caturaśraṃ vā bhūmivaśena vā caturdvāraṃ ṣaṭpathaṃ navasaṃsthānaṃ māpayeyuḥ khātavaprasāladvārāṭṭālakasampannaṃ bhaye sthāne ca | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 1.1]
madhyamasyottare navabhāge rājavāstukaṃ dhanuḥśatāyāmam ardhavistāram paścimārdhe tasyāntaḥpuram | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 2.1]
antarvaṃśikasainyaṃ cānte niviśeta | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 3.1]
purastād upasthānam dakṣiṇataḥ kośaśāsanakāryakaraṇāni vāmato rājopavāhyānāṃ hastyaśvarathānāṃ sthānam | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 4.1]
ato dhanuḥśatāntarāścatvāraḥ śakaṭamethīpratatistambhasālaparikṣepāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 5.1]
prathame purastān mantripurohitau dakṣiṇataḥ koṣṭhāgāraṃ mahānasaṃ ca vāmataḥ kupyāyudhāgāram | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 6.1]
dvitīye maulabhṛtānāṃ sthānam aśvarathānāṃ senāpateśca | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 7.1]
tṛtīye hastinaḥ śreṇyaḥ praśāstā ca | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 8.1]
caturthe viṣṭir nāyako mitrāmitrāṭavībalaṃ svapuruṣādhiṣṭhitam | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 9.1]
vaṇijo rūpājīvāścānumahāpatham | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 10.1]
bāhyato lubdhakaśvagaṇinaḥ satūryāgnayaḥ gūḍhāścārakṣāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 11.1]
śatrūṇām āpāte kūpakūṭāvapātakaṇṭakinīśca sthāpayet | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 12.1]
aṣṭādaśavargāṇām ārakṣaviparyāsaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 13.1]
divāyāmaṃ ca kārayed apasarpajñānārtham | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 14.1]
vivādasaurikasamājadyūtavāraṇaṃ ca kārayenmudrārakṣaṇaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 15.1]
senānivṛttam āyudhīyam aśāsanaṃ śūnyapālo badhnīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 16.1]
purastād adhvanaḥ samyakpraśāstā rakṣaṇāni ca | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 17.1]
yāyād vardhakiviṣṭibhyām udakāni ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 10, 1 17.2]
{ArthaŚ, 10, 2}
grāmāraṇyānām adhvani niveśān yavasendhanodakavaśena parisaṃkhyāya sthānāsanagamanakālaṃ ca yātrāṃ yāyāt | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 1.1]
tatpratīkāradviguṇaṃ bhaktopakaraṇaṃ vāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 2.1]
aśakto vā sainyeṣvāyojayet antareṣu vā nicinuyāt | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 3.1]
purastān nāyakaḥ madhye kalatraṃ svāmī ca pārśvayor aśvā bāhūtsāraḥ cakrānteṣu hastinaḥ prasāravṛddhir vā paścāt senāpatir yāyānniviśeta | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 4.1]
sarvato vanājīvaḥ prasāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 5.1]
svadeśād anvāyatir vīvadhaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 6.1]
mitrabalam āsāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 7.1]
kalatrasthānam apasāraḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 8.1]
purastād abhyāghāte makareṇa yāyāt paścācchakaṭena pārśvayor vajreṇa samantataḥ sarvatobhadreṇa ekāyane sūcyā | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 9.1]
pathidvaidhībhāve svabhūmito yāyāt | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 10.1]
abhūmiṣṭhānāṃ hi svabhūmiṣṭhā yuddhe pratilomā bhavanti | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 11.1]
yojanam adhamā adhyardhaṃ madhyamā dviyojanam uttamā sambhāvyā vā gatiḥ | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 12.1]
āśrayakārī sampannaghātī pārṣṇir āsāro madhyama udāsīno vā pratikartavyaḥ saṃkaṭo mārgaḥ śodhayitavyaḥ kośo daṇḍo mitrāmitrāṭavībalaṃ viṣṭir ṛtur vā pratīkṣyāḥ kṛtadurgakarmanicayarakṣākṣayaḥ krītabalanirvedo mitrabalanirvedaś cāgamiṣyati upajapitāro vā nātitvarayanti śatrur abhiprāyaṃ vā pūrayiṣyati iti śanair yāyāt viparyaye śīghram | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 13.1]
hastistambhasaṃkramasetubandhanaukāṣṭhaveṇusaṃghātair alābucarmakaraṇḍadṛtiplavagaṇḍikāveṇikābhiś codakāni tārayet | [ArthaŚ, 10, 2 14.1]
{ArthaŚ, 14, 1}
cāturvarṇya rakṣā artham aupaniṣadikam adharmiṣṭheṣu prayuñjīta | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465266_1]
kālakūṭa ādiḥ viṣa vargaḥ śraddheya deśa veṣa śilpa bhāṣā abhijana apadeśaiḥ kubja vāmana kirāta mūka badhira jaḍa andha chadmabhiḥ mleccha jātīyaiḥ abhipretaiḥ strībhiḥ puṃbhiḥ ca para śarīra upabhogeṣu avadhātavyaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465267_1]
rāja krīḍā bhāṇḍa nidhāna dravya upabhogeṣu gūḍhāḥ śastra nidhānam kuryuḥ sattra ājīvinaḥ ca rātri cāriṇaḥ agni jīvinaḥ ca agni nidhānam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465268_1]
citra bheka kauṇḍinyaka kṛkaṇa pañca kuṣṭha śatapadī cūrṇam śata kanda idhma kṛkalāsa cūrṇam gṛhagolikā andhāhika krakaṇṭhaka pūtikīṭa gomārikā cūrṇam sadyas prāṇa haram eteṣām _ dhūmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465269_1]

sadyas prāṇa haraḥ mataḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465271_2]

vyāghātaka mūlam bhallātaka puṣpa cūrṇa yuktam kīṭa yogaḥ māsikaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465273_1]
kalā mātram puruṣāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465274_1]
dviguṇam khara aśvānām | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465274_2]
caturguṇam hasti uṣṭrāṇām | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465274_3]
śata kardama uccidiṅga karavīra kaṭutumbī matsya dhūmaḥ madana kodrava palālena hastikarṇapalāśa palālena _ pravāta anuvāte praṇītaḥ _ carati tāvat mārayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465275_1]
pūtikīṭa matsya kaṭutumbī śata kardama idhma indragopa cūrṇam pūtikīṭa kṣudrā hema vidārī cūrṇam _ basta śṛṅga khura cūrṇa yuktam andhīkaraḥ dhūmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465276_1]
pūtikarañja pattra haritāla manaḥśilā guñjā rakta kārpāsa palālāni āsphoṭa kāca go śakṛt rasa piṣṭam andhīkaraḥ dhūmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465277_1]
sarpa nirmokam go aśva purīṣam andhāhika śiras ca andhīkaraḥ dhūmaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465278_1]
pārāvata plavaka kravyādānām hasti nara varāhānām ca mūtra purīṣam kāsīsa hiṅgu yava tuṣa kaṇa taṇḍulāḥ kārpāsa kuṭaja kośātakīnām ca bījāni gomūtrikā bhāṇḍī mūlam hasti nakha śṛṅga cūrṇam iti eṣa dhūmaḥ madana kodrava palālena hastikarṇapalāśa palālena _ praṇītaḥ pratyekaśaḥ _ carati tāvat mārayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465279_1]
kālī kuṣṭha naḍa śatāvarī mūlam sarpa pracalāka kṛkaṇa pañca kuṣṭha cūrṇam _ dhūmaḥ pūrva kalpena ārdra śuṣka palālena _ praṇītaḥ saṃgrāma avataraṇa avaskandana saṃkuleṣu kṛta nejana udaka akṣi pratīkāraiḥ praṇītaḥ sarva prāṇinām netra hanaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465280_1]
śārikā kapota baka balākā leṇḍam arka akṣi pīluka snuhī kṣīra piṣṭam andhīkaraṇam andhīkaraṇam añjanam udaka udaka dūṣaṇam dūṣaṇam ca ca | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465281_1]
yavaka śāli mūla madana phala jātī pattra nara mūtra yogaḥ plakṣa vidārī mūla yuktaḥ mūka udumbara madana kodrava kvātha yuktaḥ hastikarṇapalāśa kvātha yuktaḥ _ madana yogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465282_1]
śṛṅgi gautama vṛka kaṇṭakāra mayūra padi yogaḥ guñjā lāṅgalī viṣa mūlikā iṅguda yogaḥ madana kodrava kvātha yuktaḥ hastikarṇapalāśa kvātha yuktaḥ _ madana yogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465283_1]
samastāḥ _ yavasa indhana udaka dūṣaṇāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465284_1]

pañca kuṣṭhaka kauṇḍinyaka rājavṛkṣa puṣpa madhu yogaḥ jvara karaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465290_1]
bhāsa nakula jihvā granthikā yogaḥ kharī kṣīra piṣṭaḥ mūka badhira karaḥ māsa ārdhamāsikaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465291_1]
kalā mātram puruṣāṇām iti samānam pūrveṇa | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465292_1]
bhaṅga kvātha upanayanam auṣadhānām cūrṇam prāṇabhṛtām sarveṣām _ kvātha upanayanam evam vīryavattaram bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465293_1]
iti yoga saṃpad | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465294_1]
śālmalī vidārī dhānya siddhaḥ mūla vatsanābha saṃyuktaḥ chuchundarī śoṇita pralepeṇa digdhaḥ bāṇaḥ yam vidhyati saḥ viddhaḥ anyān daśa puruṣān daśati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465295_1]
te daṣṭāḥ daśa anyān daśanti puruṣān | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465295_2]
puṣpaiḥ elā kākṣi guggulu hālāhalānām ca kaṣāyam basta nara śoṇita yuktam daṃśa yogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465296_1]

matsya paramparā hi etena daṣṭā abhimṛṣṭā _ viṣībhavati yaḥ ca etat udakam pibati spṛśati _ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465298_1]
rakta śveta sarṣapaiḥ godhā tri pakṣa muṣṭikāyām bhūmau nikhātāyām nihitā vadhyena uddhṛtā _ paśyati tāvat mārayati kṛṣṇasarpaḥ _ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 1 465299_1]

{ArthaŚ, 14, 2}
śirīṣa udumbara śamī cūrṇam sarpiṣā saṃhṛtya ārdhamāsikaḥ kṣudh yogaḥ kaśeruka utpala kanda ikṣu mūla bisa dūrvā kṣīra ghṛta maṇḍa siddhaḥ māsikaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465311_1]
māṣa yava kulattha darbha mūla cūrṇam _ kṣīra ghṛtābhyām vallī kṣīra ghṛtam _ sama siddham sāla pṛśniparṇī mūla kalkam payasā pītvā payaḥ _ tad siddham madhu ghṛtābhyām aśitvā māsam upavasati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465313_1]
śveta basta mūtre sapta rātra uṣitaiḥ siddhārthakaiḥ siddham tailam kaṭukālābau māsa ardha māsa sthitam catuṣpada dvipadānām virūpa karaṇam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465314_1]
takra yava bhakṣasya sapta rātrāt ūrdhvam śveta gardabhasya leṇḍa yavaiḥ siddham gaurasarṣapa tailam virūpa karaṇam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465315_1]

kaṭukālābau valī gate gatam ardha māsa sthitam gaura sarṣapa piṣṭam romṇām śvetīkaraṇam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465319_1]
alojunā iti yaḥ kīṭaḥ śvetā ca gṛhagolikā etena piṣṭena abhyaktāḥ keśāḥ syuḥ śaṅkha pāṇḍarāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465321_1]

khadyota cūrṇam sarṣapa taila yuktam rātrau jvalati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465329_1]

maṇḍūka kulīra ādīnām vasayā sama bhāgam tailam siddham abhyaṅgam gātrāṇām agni prajvālanam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465336_1]

upodakī pratibalā vañjulaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ eteṣām mūla kalkena maṇḍūka vasayā saha sādhayet tailam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465341_1]

ayaskāntaḥ _ pāṣāṇaḥ kulīra dardura khārakīṭa vasā pradehena dviguṇaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465354_1]
nāraka garbhaḥ kaṅka bhāsa pārśva utpala udaka piṣṭaḥ catuṣpada dvipadānām pāda lepaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465355_1]
ulūka gṛdhra vasābhyām uṣṭra carma upānahau abhyajya vaṭapattraiḥ praticchādya pañcāśat yojanāni aśrāntaḥ gacchati śyena kaṅka kāka gṛdhra haṃsa krauñca vīcīrallāṇām majjānaḥ retāṃsi _ yojana śatāya siṃha vyāghra dvīpa kāka ulūkānām majjānaḥ retāṃsi _ sārvavarṇikāni garbha patanāni uṣṭrikāyām abhiṣūya śmaśāne śiśūn _ tad samutthitam medaḥ yojana śatāya | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465356_1]
sārvavarṇikāni | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465358_1]
aniṣṭaiḥ adbhuta utpātaiḥ parasya udvegam ācaret | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465359_1]
nirvādaḥ samānaḥ kopaḥ ucyate | [ArthaŚ, 14, 2 465360_1]
{ArthaŚ, 14, 3}
mārjāroṣṭravṛkavarāhaśvāvidvāgulīnaptṛkākolūkānām anyeṣāṃ vā niśācarāṇāṃ sattvānām ekasya dvayor bahūnāṃ vā dakṣiṇāni vāmāni cākṣīṇi gṛhītvā dvidhā cūrṇaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 1.1]
tato dakṣiṇaṃ vāmena vāmaṃ dakṣiṇena samabhyajya rātrau tamasi ca paśyati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 2.1]
ekāmlakaṃ varāhākṣi khadyotaḥ kālaśārivā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 3.1]
etenābhyaktanayano rātrau rūpāṇi paśyati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 3.2]
trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śastrahatasya śūlaprotasya vā puṃsaḥ śiraḥkapāle mṛttikāyāṃ yavān āvāsyāvikṣīreṇa secayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 4.1]
tato yavavirūḍhamālām ābadhya naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 5.1]
trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śvamārjārolūkavāgulīnāṃ dakṣiṇāni vāmāni cākṣīṇi dvidhā cūrṇaṃ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 6.1]
tato yathāsvam abhyaktākṣo naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 7.1]
trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa puruṣaghātinaḥ kāṇḍakasya śalākām añjanīṃ ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 8.1]
tato 'nyatamenākṣicūrṇenābhyaktākṣo naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 9.1]
trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa kālāyasīm añjanīṃ śalākāṃ ca kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 10.1]
tato niśācarāṇāṃ sattvānām anyatamasya śiraḥkapālam añjanena pūrayitvā mṛtāyāḥ striyā yonau praveśya dāhayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 11.1]
tad añjanaṃ puṣyeṇoddhṛtya tasyām añjanyāṃ nidadhyāt | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 12.1]
tenābhyaktākṣo naṣṭachāyārūpaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 13.1]
yatra brāhmaṇam āhitāgniṃ dagdhaṃ dahyamānaṃ vā paśyet tatra trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa svayaṃmṛtasya vāsasā prasevaṃ kṛtvā citābhasmanā pūrayitvā tam ābadhya naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 14.1]
brāhmaṇasya pretakārye yo gaur māryate tasyāsthimajjacūrṇapūrṇāhibhastrā paśūnām antardhānam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 15.1]
sarpadaṣṭasya bhasmanā pūrṇā pracalākabhastrā mṛgāṇām antardhānam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 16.1]
ulūkavāgulīpucchapurīṣajānvasthicūrṇapūrṇāhibhastrā pakṣiṇām antardhānam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 17.1]
ityaṣṭāvantardhānayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 18.1]
baliṃ vairocanaṃ vande śatamāyaṃ ca śambaram | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 19.1]
bhaṇḍīrapākaṃ narakaṃ nikumbhaṃ kumbham eva ca | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 19.2]
devalaṃ nāradaṃ vande vande sāvarṇigālavam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 20.1]
eteṣām anuyogena kṛtaṃ te svāpanaṃ mahat | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 20.2]
yathā svapantyajagarāḥ svapantyapi camūkhalāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 21.1]
tathā svapantu puruṣā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 21.2]
bhaṇḍakānāṃ sahasreṇa rathanemiśatena ca | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 22.1]
imaṃ gṛhaṃ pravekṣyāmi tūṣṇīm āsantu bhāṇḍakāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 22.2]
namaskṛtvā ca manave baddhvā śunakaphelakāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 23.1]
ye devā devalokeṣu mānuṣeṣu ca brāhmaṇāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 23.2]
adhyayanapāragāḥ siddhā ye ca kailāsatāpasāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 24.1]
etebhyaḥ sarvasiddhebhyaḥ kṛtaṃ te svāpanaṃ mahat | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 24.2]
atigacchanti ca mayyapagacchantu saṃhatāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 25.1]
alite valite manave svāhā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 26.1]
etasya prayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 27.1]
trirātropoṣitaḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ puṣyayoginyāṃ śvapākīhastād vilekhāvalekhanaṃ krīṇīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 28.1]
tanmāṣaiḥ saha kaṇḍolikāyāṃ kṛtvāsaṃkīrṇa ādahane nikhānayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 29.1]
dvitīyasyāṃ caturdaśyām uddhṛtya kumāryā peṣayitvā gulikāḥ kārayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 30.1]
tata ekāṃ gulikām abhimantrayitvā yatraitena mantreṇa kṣipati tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 31.1]
etenaiva kalpena śvāvidhaḥ śalyakaṃ trikālaṃ triśvetam asaṃkīrṇa ādahane nikhānayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 32.1]
dvitīyasyāṃ caturdaśyām uddhṛtyādahanabhasmanā saha yatraitena mantreṇa kṣipati tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 33.1]
suvarṇapuṣpīṃ brahmāṇīṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca kuśadhvajam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 34.1]
sarvāśca devatā vande vande sarvāṃśca tāpasān | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 34.2]
vaśaṃ me brāhmaṇā yāntu bhūmipālāśca kṣatriyāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 35.1]
vaśaṃ vaiśyāśca śūdrāśca vaśatāṃ yāntu me sadā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 35.2]
svāhā amile kimile vayucāre prayoge phakke vayuhve vihāle dantakaṭake svāhā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 36.1]
sukhaṃ svapantu śunakā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 37.1]
śvāvidhaḥ śalyakaṃ caitat triśvetaṃ brahmanirmitam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 37.2]
prasuptāḥ sarvasiddhā hi etat te svāpanaṃ kṛtam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 38.1]
yāvad grāmasya sīmāntaḥ sūryasyodgamanād iti | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 38.2]
svāhā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 39.1]
etasya prayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 40.1]
śvāvidhaḥ śalyakāni triśvetāni saptarātropoṣitaḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ khādirābhiḥ samidhābhir agnim etena mantreṇāṣṭaśatasampātaṃ kṛtvā madhughṛtābhyām abhijuhuyāt | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 41.1]
tata ekam etena mantreṇa grāmadvāri gṛhadvāri vā yatra nikhanyate tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 42.1]
baliṃ vairocanaṃ vande śatamāyaṃ ca śambaram | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 43.1]
nikumbhaṃ narakaṃ kumbhaṃ tantukacchaṃ mahāsuram | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 43.2]
armālavaṃ pramīlaṃ ca maṇḍolūkaṃ ghaṭobalam | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 44.1]
kṛṣṇakaṃsopacāraṃ ca paulomīṃ ca yaśasvinīm | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 44.2]
abhimantrayitvā gṛhṇāmi siddhyarthaṃ śavaśārikām | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 45.1]
jayatu jayati ca namaḥ śalakabhūtebhyaḥ svāhā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 45.2]
sukhaṃ svapantu śunakā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 46.1]

yāvad astam ayād udayo yāvadarthaṃ phalaṃ mama | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 46.3]
iti svāhā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 47.1]
etasya prayogaḥ | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 48.1]
caturbhaktopavāsī kṛṣṇacaturdaśyām asaṃkīrṇa ādahane baliṃ kṛtvaitena mantreṇa śavaśārikāṃ gṛhītvā pautrīpoṭṭalikaṃ badhnīyāt | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 49.1]
tanmadhye śvāvidhaḥ śalyakena viddhvā yatraitena mantreṇa nikhanyate tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 50.1]
upaimi śaraṇaṃ cāgniṃ daivatāni diśo daśa | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 51.1]
apayāntu ca sarvāṇi vaśatāṃ yāntu me sadā | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 51.2]

trirātropoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śarkarā ekaviṃśatisampātaṃ kṛtvā madhughṛtābhyām abhijuhuyāt | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 54.1]
tato gandhamālyena pūjayitvā nikhānayet | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 55.1]

dvigoyuktaṃ goyānam āhṛtaṃ bhavati | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 59.1]

tālodghāṭanaṃ prasvāpanaṃ ca | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 63.1]

eteṣām ekaḥ purīṣe mūtre vā nikhāta ānāhaṃ karoti pade 'syāsane vā nikhātaḥ śoṣeṇa mārayati āpaṇe kṣetre gṛhe vā vṛtticchedaṃ karoti | [ArthaŚ, 14, 3 71.1]
